Balanced coupled composition (Track CD, v2.0.39): cross-center V_ne via multipole expansion of 1/|r-R_B|, terminates exactly at L_max=2*l_max by Gaunt selection rules. LiH at n_max=2: 878 Pauli terms (2.63├Ś composed, Conjecture 1 confirmed), 74.1 Ha 1-norm (1.98├Ś), 87 QWC groups. 4-electron FCI: 1.8% energy error, 7.0% R_eq error, only bound configuration (decoupled 10.9%, PK 15.0%, CB 29.0% ŌĆö all unbound). D_e=0.037 Ha. Key files: `geovac/shibuya_wulfman.py` (compute_cross_center_vne), `geovac/balanced_coupled.py` (build_balanced_hamiltonian). Phase 4A with analytical V_ne integrals (incomplete gamma, machine precision): n_max=3 E(3.015)=-8.055 Ha (0.20% error). R_eq=3.280 bohr (8.8% error, structural drift +0.053 bohr/n_max, 3x smaller than PK). MIXED: energy converges excellently, R_eq drifts structurally. Optimal for single-point quantum simulation at fixed geometries. Nested hyperspherical investigation (Track DF, v2.5.0, 6 sprints): H-set coupled angular basis on S^(3N-1) produces 18-26% lower ERI density than uncoupled basis via 6j recoupling zeros (novel sparsity mechanism). Compact encoding: Q=10 for 4-electron systems (3├Ś fewer qubits than composed Q=12), comparable Pauli count (112 vs 115), 6.4├Ś lower 1-norm for atoms (PK elimination). Molecular extension: NEGATIVE for all three approaches (single-center R_eq 33.7%, charge-center 48.2% energy error, heterogeneous L├Čwdin destroys sparsity 1,711 vs 120 Pauli terms). Composed architecture confirmed as structurally necessary for molecular PES. Key files: `geovac/nested_hyperspherical.py`, `tests/test_nested_hyperspherical.py`. Precision atomic spectra (Track DI, v2.6.0, Sprint 1): 2D variational solver on SŌüĄ eliminates adiabatic approximation. Tensor-product basis: spectral Laguerre (R) ├Ś spectral Gegenbauer (╬▒), treating hyperradius and hyperangle simultaneously. Breaks the adiabatic 0.19-0.20% floor: raw 0.022% at l_max=7 (n_basis_R=25, n_basis_alpha=40). With Schwartz cusp correction at l_max=4: 0.004% error (E=-2.90383 Ha vs exact -2.90372 Ha). Phase 1 target (<0.01%) achieved. Adiabatic floor was structural to the Born-Oppenheimer-like separation of R and ╬▒; the 2D solver captures the full R-╬▒ correlation. l_max convergence is monotonic with ~l^{-2} rate (dominated by per-channel angular basis quality, not partial-wave truncation per se). Key files: `geovac/level3_variational.py` (solve_he_variational_2d, solve_he_precision), `tests/test_level3_variational.py` (17 tests), `debug/data/track_di_he_variational_2d.json`. Algebraic Casimir CI (Track DI, v2.6.0, Sprint 2): Fully algebraic FCI matrix H(k) = Bk + Ck┬▓ with exact rational Slater integrals from Paper 7's S┬│ formula. 21 F^k + 14 G^k integrals verified symbolically. n_max=1: k*=27/16, E*=-729/256 (exact rationals, 1.93%). n_max=3: E*=-2.860 Ha (1.50%, 31 configurations). Self-consistency k┬▓=-2E: NEGATIVE (over-constrains 2-electron problem, 5-13% error; variational k is always better). Three-layer structure: rational (Slater integrals) ŌåÆ algebraic (optimal exponents) ŌåÆ transcendental (e-e cusp). Off-diagonal one-body elements (k-Z)Ō¤©a|1/r|bŌ¤® required for variational bound. Key files: `geovac/casimir_ci.py` (build_fci_matrix, solve_self_consistent, solve_variational), `tests/test_casimir_ci.py` (32 tests), `debug/data/track_di_casimir_ci.json`. Graph-native CI (Track DI, v2.6.0, Sprint 3C): Graph Laplacian hŌéü + rational Slater V_ee, zero free parameters. He ground state 0.19% at n_max=7 (1,218 configs). Beats FCI-A paper (0.22% vs 0.35% at n_max=5) due to exact rational integrals replacing 2000-pt grid numerics. Graph off-diagonal hŌéü accounts for 86% of CI correlation energy ŌĆö the topology is the dominant ingredient. Three-sequence comparison: graph-native (0.19%) >> variational-k (1.41%) >> fixed-k=Z (1.85%). Key files: `geovac/casimir_ci.py` (build_graph_native_fci, _build_graph_h1), `debug/data/track_di_graph_native.json`. Basis invariance verification (Track DI, v2.6.0, Sprint 3D): FCI is invariant under orbital rotation ŌĆö transforming V_ee to the graph eigenbasis gives identical energies (< 3├Ś10Ōü╗┬╣ŌüĄ Ha) at n_max=1-4. The ~0.14% convergence floor is NOT from basis mismatch between graph hŌéü and hydrogenic V_ee. Floor is from cusp + finite-n_max truncation (embedding exchange constant content, Paper 18). Three-layer structure refined: rational (graph hŌéü + Slater V_ee, 98.6% of exact) ŌåÆ topological (T┬▒ inter-shell couplings via ╬║=-1/16, dominant one-body correlation) ŌåÆ transcendental (cusp, ~0.14% floor). Key files: `geovac/casimir_ci.py` (build_graph_consistent_fci), `tests/test_casimir_ci.py` (38 tests), `debug/data/track_di_graph_consistent.json`.

**RH sprint: GeoVac Hopf graphs are strictly Ramanujan (v2.20.0, April 17, 2026):** Ihara zeta computed on the S┬│ Coulomb graph (Paper 7) and SŌüĄ Bargmann-Segal graph (Paper 24) via the Ihara-Bass determinantal formula and the 2E ├Ś 2E Hashimoto non-backtracking edge operator. All four graphs tested (S┬│ at max_n=2,3; SŌüĄ at N_max=2,3) satisfy the Kotani-Sunada Ramanujan bound **strictly**: largest non-trivial Hashimoto eigenvalue sits strictly inside ŌłÜq_max. Deviations: S┬│ max_n=3: ŌłÆ0.198; SŌüĄ N_max=2: ŌłÆ0.208; SŌüĄ N_max=3: ŌłÆ0.357 (strongly Ramanujan). Closed forms are integer-coefficient polynomial factorizations: S┬│ at max_n=3 decomposes per Ōäō-shell (Fock adjacency preserves Ōäō); SŌüĄ at N_max=3 factors as (s┬▒1)┬▓┬│┬ĘP_12(s┬▓)┬ĘP_22(s┬▓), a 12+22 dichotomy conjecturally matching Paper 25's Hopf-U(1) block decomposition (untested). No transcendentals (ŽĆ, ╬Č(2), ╬Č(3)) in any zero ŌĆö Paper 24's ŽĆ-free certificate extends from adjacency to Ihara zeta. Standard Stark-Terras single-critical-circle functional equation does NOT hold (graphs are irregular); what does hold is sŌåÆŌłÆs reflection and Galois closure. Parallel Wick-rotation investigation (Track RH-B, memo at `debug/fock_continuation_memo.md`) is a clean negative: Fock's S┬│ŌåÆH┬│ continuation (Bander-Itzykson 1966) is clean but provides no discrete ╬ō ŌŖé SO(3,1) from framework invariants ŌĆö Weyl of SO(4) is not a lattice, Hopf S┬╣ irrelevant for H┬│, Bianchi PSL(2, O_K) selected by no GeoVac invariant (Rydberg, pŌéĆ=Z/n, ╬║=ŌłÆ1/16, B=42, F=ŽĆ┬▓/6, ╬ö=1/40, ╬▒). Universal/Coulomb partition sharpened three ways: S┬│ discrete Hopf calibration-ŽĆ, SŌüĄ holomorphic ŽĆ-free, H┬│ continuous no-╬ō. Graph-zeta is the single RH-adjacent direction intrinsic to GeoVac; Selberg-on-hydrogen is structurally closed. Paper 29 drafted (`papers/group1_operator_algebras/paper_29_ramanujan_hopf.tex`). Literature survey (`debug/rh_literature_survey.md`, 60 entries) confirmed RH-A is not duplicated in the literature to Jan 2026; spectrum-as-zeros is ruled out for our integer Dirac spectrum (Berry-Tabor + Odlyzko) ŌĆö any RH bridge must go through graph zeta or derived operators. Key files: `geovac/ihara_zeta.py`, `tests/test_ihara_zeta.py` (15/15 passing), `debug/ihara_zeta_memo.md`, `debug/data/ihara_zeta_geovac_hopf.json`. **RH-C follow-up (same sprint, v2.20.0):** Spin-ful Ihara zeta extension onto the Dirac-S┬│ graph (nodes labeled by DiracLabel (n_fock, ╬║, m_j) from `geovac/dirac_matrix_elements.py`). Two adjacency rules computed: Rule A (╬║-preserving, direct lift of scalar Fock ladders) and Rule B (E1 dipole, parity-flip ╬öl=┬▒1, mixes ╬║). Both rules Ramanujan at n_max=1,2,3. The ZŌéé is the only sub-action of the Paper 25 Hopf U(1) that commutes with a real integer adjacency; the continuous U(1) phase rotation reduces to this ZŌéé on real data. Verified symbolically: det(M_sym) = (sŌłÆ1)(s+1)┬ĘP_22 on the 13-dim symmetric block (scalar SŌüĄ); det(M_antisym) = P_12 on the 7-dim antisymmetric block; product equals full det(M). The GeoVac Hopf graphs are bipartite, so tr(T^L)=0 for odd L ŌĆö Ihara walk-length spectrum supported only on even integers. Paper 28's Žć_ŌłÆ4 Dirichlet character has support only on odd integers, so Žć_ŌłÆ4-twisted Ihara zeta is identically trivial. **Paper 28's Žć_ŌłÆ4 structure lives on the SPECTRAL zeta D(s) = ╬Ż g_n┬Ę|╬╗_n|^{ŌłÆs} (Dirac Dirichlet series at quarter-integer Hurwitz shifts), NOT on the Ihara side**. Any bridge to classical Riemann ╬Č(s) must go through the spectral zeta, not the Ihara zeta. **Classical solver details ŌĆö active frontier items (resolved or characterized):**
- l-dependent PK pseudopotential for LiH composed geometry: reduces R_eq error from 6.9% to 5.3% at l_max=2 (higher l_max with channel-blind PK diverges ŌĆö see Section 3). **l_max divergence root cause confirmed (Track BQ, v2.0.32): NOT from adiabatic approximation.** Variational 2D solver (level4_method='variational_2d') produces identical drift: R_eq = 3.18, 3.33, 3.63 bohr at l_max=2,3,4 (+0.15-0.22 bohr/l_max). Single-point E(R=3.015) also diverges: -8.184, -8.204, -8.236 Ha (exact: -8.071), violating variational bound ŌĆö PK overcounting worsens with angular channels. CBS extrapolation: R_eqŌåÆ3.73 bohr (24% error). Root cause is structural to PK/composed architecture: higher-l channels interact with the l-dependent PK barrier in ways that systematically overcount correlation. **l_max=2 is the optimal operating point** ŌĆö higher l_max degrades both R_eq and single-point energy. Diagnostic arc (v2.0.5) confirmed: divergence is linear (+0.23 bohr/l_max), angular spreading is 100% nuclear. R-dependent PK w_PK(R) = ╬┤_{l,0} ├Ś min(cap, R/R_ref) achieves 2.0% at l_max=4 but requires empirical R_ref. Ab initio R_ref derivation attempted (Track AD, v2.0.18): all core-derived candidates (core radius, PK width, screening length: 0.27-0.82 bohr) too small to affect PES ŌĆö R_ref needs to be molecular-scale (~3 bohr) but no atomic property bridges this gap without circular reasoning. Negative result.
- Polyatomic PES: BeH2 full 1-RDM exchange achieves 11.7% R_eq error (down from 20% diagonal S┬ĘFŌü░, matches 12% fitted model with zero free parameters). Kinetic orthogonalization tested: +0.03 Ha uniform, no R_eq effect (negative result). Remaining 11.7% attributed to basis truncation (l_max=2) and PK structural overcounting (NOT adiabatic approximation ŌĆö see Track BQ).
- HŌééO composed solver: 5-block architecture (O 1s┬▓ core + 2 OŌĆōH bond pairs + 2 lone pairs), R_eq 26% error with charge-center origin. Coupling architecture validated (bond-bond ~0.5 Ha, consistent with BeHŌéé), but lone pair coupling unphysical at Z_eff=6 (S┬ĘFŌü░ produces ŌłÆ28 Ha bond-lone, ŌłÆ15 Ha lone-lone ŌĆö exceeds total electronic energy). Bottleneck is Level 4 angular basis at 6:1 charge asymmetry (R_eq error scales: 0.1% at 1:1, 18% at 2:1, 17% at 6:1 with charge-center).
- Algebraic audit confirmed: Level 4 nuclear coupling (Paper 15) uses split-region Legendre expansion with Gaunt integrals ŌĆö not quadrature. Core screening (Paper 17) has algebraic density from channel coefficients. Paper 15 Section V.A corrected to match production code.
- Chemical periodicity as representation theory (Paper 16) -- computational exploitation of hierarchical structure

**Completed investigation tracks (v2.0.6-23) ŌĆö see CHANGELOG.md for full details:**

The classical solver investigation comprised 30+ tracks across four phases. Key structural findings by phase:

*Spectral solvers and coupled-channel infrastructure (v2.0.6-11, Tracks A-K):* Replaced FD solvers with spectral bases at Levels 2-4, achieving 100-269├Ś dimension reductions. Algebraic Laguerre matrix elements at Levels 2-3 (zero quadrature for m=0; single transcendental seed e^a┬ĘEŌéü(a) for mŌēĀ0). Level 3 coupled-channel convergence ceiling 0.19-0.20% (adiabatic truncation). Perturbation series definitive negative (branch point obstruction). 2D solver integrated into composed pipeline.

*Algebraicization (v2.0.12-13, Tracks N-S):* Level 3 eigenvalues ╬╝(R) proven algebraic over Q(ŽĆ,ŌłÜ2), not transcendental. Level 4 angular Hamiltonian structurally non-algebraic (piecewise-smooth). Algebraic Z_eff and Slater integrals wired as production defaults.

*Cusp attack (v2.0.14-16, Tracks U-Y):* Three negative results (alpha-only cusp factor, graph absorption of 1/rŌéüŌéé, ╬ĖŌéüŌéé-adapted basis) ŌĆö cusp is 2D in (╬▒, ╬ĖŌéüŌéé), not separable. One positive: Schwartz partial-wave extrapolation breaks through 0.19-0.20% floor (He: 0.10% at l_max=2).

*Channel convergence and diagnostics (v2.0.17-18, Tracks Z-AD):* Level 4 convergence through l_max=6: 96.0% D_e, CBS ~97%. Even-odd staircase is selection rule physics (gerade constraint). Geometric elevation structurally irreducible (three avenues negative). PK essential for equilibrium; R_ref derivation failed (scale mismatch).

*Full N-electron architecture (v2.0.19-23, Tracks AF-AS):* Built full 4-electron solver (Level 4N) as exact validation. Equilibrium exists without PK at l_maxŌēź2. All radial solvers exhausted. Angular basis is bottleneck: l_max=2 SŌéä [2,2] has 12 channels vs composed geometry's 144├Ś compression at 5.3% R_eq. Composed quantum encoding categorically sparser (334 vs 3,288 Pauli terms, 20├Ś lower 1-norm).

(e) Resolvent: (63/4)┬ĘŽĆ┬Ęcoth(ŽĆ) Ōēł 49.67 (13.8% gap from B+F). **The Phase 4D structural conclusion is the strongest result of the alpha sprint series so far:** F = ŽĆ┬▓/6 CANNOT enter K through any Hopf-fiber trace, discrete OR continuous. The Jacobi inversion mechanism systematically lowers the ŽĆ power by ┬Į at each order, which explains both Phase 4C's all-rational fiber zetas (no ŽĆ at all in finite path graphs) and Phase 4D's all-linear-ŽĆ asymptotics (ŽĆ but never ŽĆ┬▓). - Sommerfeld fine-structure Dirichlet sums DŌééŌĆōDŌéå (v2.26.1): exact closed-form coefficients c_p(n) extracted from the Dirac-Coulomb energy expansion through order (Z╬▒)┬╣┬▓, verified symbolically for n=1..15 at each order. - **QED STRATEGIC DIRECTIVE (2026-04-27, refined 2026-05-03): ALGEBRAIC-FIRST.** New QED investigation work should reach for closed-form / algebraic structure before scaling up numerical convergence loops. The original directive was framed as "graph-native first" because graph-native is exact at every n_max in ŌäÜ[ŌłÜd] (d square-free) ŌĆö it's the cleanest place sub-agents can land on closed forms, and the c3 coefficient sprint (n_int=50 with Richardson extrapolation for ~3 significant digits) was the cautionary case. But the discipline generalizes: sometimes the closed form is in continuum (Sommerfeld D_p Hurwitz expressions, the two-term Dirac heat kernel exactness theorem on S┬│, the K-CC algebraic obstruction via T9). The wrong move is cranking n_int, n_max, or basis size for marginal precision when an algebraic structure is reachable ŌĆö that wastes sub-agent budget and produces digit-precision answers when the actual question is structural. Stop, find the structure, then compute. Graph-native and continuum are complementary tools: graph-native often gives structure cleanly (pendant-edge theorem, 1+6+1 partition, FŌéé even-rationality, ŽĆ-free certificates), continuum sometimes gives precision cleanly (Lamb shift sub-percent closure, Sommerfeld D_p coefficients, two-loop bracket prefactors). The exchange-constant taxonomy (Paper 18) and projection taxonomy (Paper 34) are the dictionaries that say which representation owns which question. Both layers of QED infrastructure remain available; the discipline is choosing which to invoke for the question at hand. PM responsibility: when dispatching a sub-agent, name the algebraic structure being targeted (closed form, ring, theorem), not just "compute X to higher precision."
- Graph-native QED on the finite Fock graph (v2.26.1, Tracks GN-1 through GN-7): seven modules implementing QED entirely on the finite GeoVac graph using exact rational/algebraic arithmetic. **All graph-native QED quantities are ŽĆ-free** ŌĆö live in ŌäÜ[ŌłÜ2, ŌłÜ3, ŌłÜ6, ...] (algebraic integers from CG coefficients), not ŌäÜ. Key results: (1) Fock graph Hodge decomposition verified (GN-1, `geovac/fock_graph_hodge.py`); (2) electron propagator G_e = DŌü╗┬╣ in the Dirac (n,╬║,m_j) basis (GN-2, `geovac/graph_qed_propagator.py`); (3) photon propagator G_╬│ = LŌéüŌü║ and VP as finite matrix trace (GN-3, `geovac/graph_qed_photon.py`); (4) vertex coupling tensor V[a,b,e] via CG projection (GN-4, `geovac/graph_qed_vertex.py`); (5) self-energy ╬Ż with Tr=44/3 at n_max=2, positive semidefinite, 5 zero eigenvalues matching photon kernel (GN-5, `geovac/graph_qed_self_energy.py`); (6) vertex correction ╬ø with Tr=32/9, anomalous moment FŌéé=5ŌłÜ2/3 Ōēł 2.357 (irrational but ŽĆ-free); (7) **broken structural zero**: Paper 28 Theorem 4 (╬Ż(n_ext=0)=0 by vertex parity) does NOT hold on the finite graph ŌĆö **pendant-edge theorem: ╬Ż(GS) = 2(n_max-1)/n_max ŌåÆ 2** exactly. The ground state vŌéĆ=|1,0,0Ō¤® is a leaf node (pendant vertex) at all n_max; the unique edge eŌéĆ connecting it to the graph decouples in LŌéü, giving G_╬│[eŌéĆ,eŌéĆ] = (n_max-1)/n_max via path-graph Laplacian inverse. Two continuum protection mechanisms are both absent: (a) vertex parity (nŌéü+nŌéé+q odd) requires vector photon quantum numbers, (b) SO(4) channel count W(0,n_int,q)=0 requires the photon to carry SU(2)_L├ŚSU(2)_R vector structure. **Graph computes scalar QED; vector structure is calibration** (see scalar_vs_vector_qed.md); (8) VP at n_max=3 decomposes by l-sector (l=0: 2├Ś2, l=1: 7├Ś7, l=2: 4├Ś4) with zero cross-block coupling (GN-6, `tests/test_graph_qed_nmax3.py`); (9) **projection exchange constant is RATIONAL** at every finite truncation ŌĆö C = 50471424/1779441125 at n_max=3 ŌĆö confirming Paper 18 CALIBRATION tier (GN-7, `geovac/graph_qed_continuum_bridge.py`); (10) graph captures ~35├Ś more VP content than continuum W-weighted formula at n_max=3. **Neumann/Born series for the electron propagator:** the Dirac graph operator D = ╬ø + tA decomposes into diagonal eigenvalue matrix ╬ø and sparse adjacency A; G_e(t) = ╬øŌü╗┬╣ ╬Ż_{kŌēź0} (-t┬Ę╬øŌü╗┬╣A)^k terminates exactly at order N-1 (Cayley-Hamilton), making FŌéé(t) a rational function of t over ŌäÜ(ŌłÜ2,ŌłÜ3,ŌłÜ6); spectral radius Žü(╬øŌü╗┬╣A) ~ 0.2 at t=╬║=-1/16 guarantees rapid convergence of the Born series; first-order perturbation theory already captures FŌéé to within ~0.2%. Implemented as production path in `graph_qed_propagator.py`. Paper 28 updated with new ┬¦Graph-Native QED. - Graph-native QED three-track sprint (v2.26.1, April 2026): FŌéé rational structure, selection rule census, and self-energy gap analysis. **Track 1 ŌĆö FŌéé(t) is an EVEN rational function** of the hopping coupling t, degree 2/2 over ŌäÜ(ŌłÜ2,ŌłÜ3,ŌłÜ6) at n_max=2. Notable invariants: Tr(╬Ż)/Tr(╬ø) = 33/8; tadpole = 16ŌłÜ2/15; bubble = 32/9; triangle = 3584ŌłÜ2/3375. **Track 3 ŌĆö C ├Ś FŌéé NEGATIVE RESULT:** C├ŚFŌéé grows with n_max (0.053 at n=3, 0.075 at n=4), diverging from ╬▒/(2ŽĆ) = 1.16├Ś10Ōü╗┬│. The VP projection constant C is NOT the correct projection for the vertex correction. Different diagram topologies require different spectral-density factors for the graph-to-continuum projection. C(4) = 48613183465472/1024864407042525. Self-energy gap: graph ╬Ż uniformly ~10├Ś larger than continuum (missing SO(4) W=0 suppression). - Graph-native QED FŌéé convergence sprint (v2.26.1, April 2026): Extended FŌéé computation from n_max=2..4 to n_max=2..6 using numpy (bypassing sympy eigenvalue bug at n_maxŌēź4). **FŌéé(╬║) table:** 2.353 (n=2), 1.873 (n=3), 1.589 (n=4), 1.396 (n=5), 1.253 (n=6). **Power-law convergence:** FŌéé ~ 3.507 ├Ś n^(-0.573), R┬▓ = 0.99990; local exponents increasing monotonically (-0.562 ŌåÆ -0.591). Richardson extrapolation: F_inf ~ -0.22 (unphysical ŌåÆ confirms FŌéé ŌåÆ 0 as n_max ŌåÆ Ōł×). **Rational function structure:** n_max=2 degree 2/2 over ŌäÜ(ŌłÜ2,ŌłÜ3,ŌłÜ6); n_max=3 degree 16/16 over ŌäÜ(ŌłÜ2,ŌłÜ3,ŌłÜ5,ŌłÜ6,ŌłÜ10,ŌłÜ15); Taylor coefficients at n_max=3 all negative for kŌēź2 (better convergence than n_max=2's alternating signs). **FŌéé(╬║) vs FŌéé(0) sign flip** at n_max=5 (zero-crossing of the difference; both sequences track within <0.1%). **Pendant-edge theorem** ╬Ż(GS) = 2(n_max-1)/n_max verified exactly at all 5 tested n_max (mechanism: GS is pendant vertex, G_╬│[eŌéĆ,eŌéĆ] = (n_max-1)/n_max from path-graph Laplacian inverse). **Self-energy trace scaling:** Tr(╬Ż)/N_dirac grows sublinearly (1.47 ŌåÆ 3.23 across n_max=2..6). **Successive ratios** FŌéé(n+1)/FŌéé(n) increasing toward 1: 0.796, 0.849, 0.878, 0.898 (consistent with slow power-law). - Native Dirac graph QED (v2.26.1, April 2026): QED built directly on the (n,╬║,m_j) Dirac graph, bypassing the CG projection used in the scalar Fock graph QED (GN-1 through GN-7). Two adjacency rules tested: Rule A (╬║-preserving, spinor lift of scalar ladders) and Rule B (E1 dipole, ╬öl=┬▒1 parity flip). **HEADLINE: Rule B Dirac graph recovers 4/8 continuum QED selection rules** (vs 1/8 on scalar Fock graph). Selection rules partition cleanly into three categories: (1) **Always survives (1):** Gaunt/CG sparsity; (2) **Spinor-recoverable (3):** ╬öm_j conservation (both rules), spatial parity E1 (Rule B only), Furry's theorem (both rules) ŌĆö fixed by using Dirac nodes instead of scalar Fock nodes; (3) **Vector-photon-required (4):** vertex parity, SO(4) channel count, Ward identity, charge conjugation ŌĆö require promoting photon from scalar 1-cochain to vector harmonic. **GS is NOT pendant on either Dirac graph** ŌĆö degree 2 (Rule A) and degree 5 (Rule B), constant across n_max=2,3,4. Structural zero ╬Ż(GS)=0 NOT recovered; ╬Ż is strictly positive definite (no zero eigenvalues, unlike scalar graph's 5 zeros). Exact algebraic eigenvalues: Tr(╬Ż_A) = 17/2, Tr(╬Ż_B) = 103/20; GS blocks: Rule A diag(5/8,5/8), Rule B [[103/160,21/160],[21/160,103/160]]. All quantities ŽĆ-free in ŌäÜ[ŌłÜ2,ŌłÜ17,ŌłÜ41,ŌłÜ881] ŌĆö algebraic content SIMPLER than scalar Fock (ŌäÜ[ŌłÜ2] for Rule A vs ŌäÜ[ŌłÜ2,ŌłÜ3,ŌłÜ6]). Furry's theorem recovered because identity vertex on Dirac graph is off-diagonal (odd under graph-transposition). The Dirac graph is an **intermediate construction** between scalar Fock (1/8 rules) and continuum vector QED (8/8 rules). Paper 18 classification: spinor-recoverable rules are INTRINSIC to spinor quantum numbers; vector-required rules are CALIBRATION content from the continuum embedding. - GN-QED Spectral-Zeta Projection Sprint (v2.26.1, April 2026): Three-track sprint characterizing the graph-to-continuum projection for QED on S┬│. **Track 1 ŌĆö Per-mode topological gap:** The graph-to-continuum self-energy ratio Žü(n_ext, n_int) varies from 0 to 1.66 with no clean pattern. Root cause: Fock graph has nearest-neighbor connectivity (╬ön=┬▒1 only) while continuum SO(4) channel count W obeys a triangle inequality allowing non-nearest-neighbor contributions, creating fundamental zero/nonzero asymmetries. **Track 2 ŌĆö Catalan connection CLEAN NEGATIVE:** 24 PSLQ targets against {G, ╬▓(4), ŽĆ┬▓, ╬Č(3)} all returned null. The ŽćŌéŗŌéä Dirichlet character mechanism that produces Catalan's G in the continuum is NOT accessible from finite-graph parity decomposition. Graph even/odd ratios alternate with n_max (driven by degeneracy counting); continuum ratios converge to ~1. Number field shift: FŌéé_full Ōłł ŌäÜ(ŌłÜ2) but FŌéé_even/FŌéé_odd Ōłł ŌäÜ(ŌłÜ3). **Track 3 ŌĆö Two-tier calibration structure:** Three independent projection constants C_VP, C_SE, C_F2 have structurally independent power-law scaling: C_VP ~ n^0.93 (vertex-based) or n^1.48 (photon-propagator), C_SE ~ n^1.48, C_F2 ~ n^0.57. **VP/SE constant ratio: C_VP/C_SE = 0.1035 ┬▒ 0.0009 (CV=0.83%, closest rational 3/29 = 0.10345)** ŌĆö VP and SE share the same power-law exponent, differing only by a constant ~1/10 prefactor. C_F2 exponent (+0.57) matches FŌéé convergence exponent (ŌłÆ0.57) with opposite sign, so C_F2 ├Ś FŌéé ŌåÆ ╬▒/(2ŽĆ) by construction. Two-tier structure: (a) VP/SE shared tier with exponent ~1.48 and constant ratio 3/29; (b) vertex tier with exponent ~0.57. Paper 28 updated with three-diagram projection table, VP/SE ratio finding, and new open question. - Vector QED sprint on the Fock graph (VQ-1 through VQ-5, v2.26.1, May 2026): systematic five-track investigation testing whether the 4 vector-photon-required selection rules can be recovered from the graph's intrinsic geometry without promoting the photon to a vector harmonic. **All five tracks NEGATIVE for selection rule recovery.** (VQ-1) Žā┬ĘL decomposition ŌåÆ zero on all graph edges (intra-shell only). (VQ-2) pure Žā_╬╝ vertex ŌåÆ disconnected graph (2/8 rules, worse than Dirac Rule B baseline). (VQ-3) Žā_╬╝ ŌŖŚ V_scalar vertex ŌåÆ trivial 3├Ś rescaling by Pauli trace identity ╬Ż_╬╝ Žā_╬╝┬▓ = 3I; Tr(╬Ż_vec) = 3 ├Ś Tr(╬Ż_scalar) = 44; FŌéé_vec = 3 ├Ś FŌéé_scalar = 5ŌłÜ2; number field ŌäÜ(ŌłÜ2) unchanged; breaks ╬öm_j and Furry compared to scalar; selection rules 1/8. (VQ-4) Direction-resolved Hodge decomposition: T-channel (radial, ╬ön=┬▒1) and L-channel (angular, ╬öm=┬▒1) edges classified with per-channel sub-Laplacians. **POSITIVE STRUCTURAL**: T/L spectra are anisotropic (T eigenvalues {2.0} vs L {1.0, 3.0} at n_max=2); propagator block-diagonal at n_max=2, cross-channel coupled at n_max=3 (||G_TL||/||G_full|| = 5.8%). Gives scalar photon effective "polarization" from pure topology. (VQ-5) Full vector QED combining direction channels with Žā vertex: all 15 Žā-to-channel configurations tested (5 named + exhaustive 3├Ś3 scan). Three distinct FŌéé values (1.0├Ś, 1.4├Ś, 1.6├Ś scalar), but ALL produce 1/8 surviving selection rules. **Structural conclusion:** the 4 vector-required rules (vertex parity, SO(4) channel count, Ward identity, charge conjugation) require the PHOTON to carry (L, M_L) quantum numbers ŌĆö neither spin matrices at the vertex, nor direction-resolved edges, nor their combination suffices. Confirms the three-tier selection rule partition (1 always survives, 3 spinor-recoverable, 4 vector-required) from a complementary direction. Žā-vertex approaches are now definitively closed (5 independent negatives). Paper 28 updated with new ┬¦VQ sprint subsection. - Transverse photon sector from Wilson plaquettes (v2.26.1, May 2026): Paper 30's SU(2) Wilson gauge plaquettes define 2-cells (faces) whose boundary operator dŌéü gives the co-exact Laplacian LŌéü^co = dŌéüdŌéüßĄĆ. The transverse photon propagator G_T = (dŌéüdŌéüßĄĆ)Ōü║ recovers the continuum GS structural zero ╬Ż(n_ext=0) = 0 that was broken on the scalar Fock graph (pendant-edge theorem: ╬Ż_scalar(GS) = 2(n_max-1)/n_max). **Mechanism: pendant-edge exclusion from plaquettes** ŌĆö the GS is a pendant vertex (degree 1), its unique edge eŌéĆ cannot participate in any closed walk, so dŌéü[eŌéĆ,:] = 0 and G_T[eŌéĆ,:] = 0. Verified to machine precision at n_max=3,4. **Mode-resolved analysis (STRUCTURAL NEGATIVE for remaining 3 rules):** co-exact eigenvalues approach continuum n(n+2) for lower modes, but eigenvectors have wrong SUPPORT ŌĆö confined to adjacent shell-pairs (|╬ön|Ōēż1) by graph connectivity. Triangle inequality test: modes q=3,4 PASS at n_max=4 but modes q=5,6 FAIL (63-86% violations). Ward identity: ||[╬Ż_T, HŌéĆ]||/||╬Ż_T|| Ōēł 0.58 (far from zero). **Final selection rule partition: 1 always survives (Gaunt/CG) + 3 spinor-recoverable (Dirac graph) + 1 plaquette-recoverable (GS structural zero) + 3 vector-quantum-number-required (SO(4) channel count, Ward identity, charge conjugation).** The 5/8 graph-intrinsic ratio is maximal without promoting photon 1-cochains to vector bundle sections. Paper 18 Tier 1/2 boundary precisely located: topological (eigenvalues + pendant exclusion) vs geometric (angular momentum labels on fiber). - Vector-photon QED on the Fock graph (v2.26.1, May 2026): Adding explicit photon quantum numbers (q, m_q) with Wigner 3j vertex coupling recovers **7/8 continuum QED selection rules for scalar electrons and 8/8 for Dirac electrons**. Construction: photon modes (q=1..q_max, m_q=-q..q), propagator G_╬│(q) = 1/[q(q+2)] (vector Laplacian on S┬│), vertex V(a,b,q,m_q) = 3j ├Ś parity(l_a+l_b+q odd) ├Ś R=1. Self-energy ╬Ż(a,c) = ╬Ż_{b,q,m_q} V┬ĘG_e┬ĘG_╬│┬ĘV. **Pre-investigation:** LŌéü = B^T B does NOT block-diagonalize by (q, m_q) ŌĆö photon quantum numbers are transition labels (difference between endpoint labels), not conserved at vertices. Cross-sector Frobenius fraction: 20% (Fock), 57% (Dirac Rule B). Vector photon structure must be added from outside. **Selection rule census (scalar 7/8, Dirac 8/8):** Gaunt/CG sparsity PASS (built into 3j), vertex parity / GS zero PASS (l_a+l_b+q odd; GS: 2l=evenŌēĀodd), SO(4) channel count PASS (triangle inequality), ╬öm/╬öm_j conservation PASS (3j m-rule), spatial parity PASS (E1), Ward identity PASS at n_max=2 / FAIL at n_max=3 (truncation), charge conjugation PASS (╬Ż Hermiticity). **Furry's theorem: FAIL for scalar, PASS for Dirac.** For scalar electrons, V(a,a,q,m_q) is nonzero for lŌēź1 when q is odd. For Dirac electrons, the **Dirac spinor phase constraint** forces V(a,a,q,m_q) = 0 identically: the ╬▒-matrix is off-diagonal in large/small component space, and the i-factor on the small component of Žł = (f┬Ę╬®_╬║, ig┬Ę╬®_{ŌłÆ╬║}) makes V_LS + V_SL = 0 by Hermiticity. This is a KINEMATIC identity of the single-particle Dirac vertex, NOT the field-theoretic C-symmetry mechanism. **GS structural zero:** ╬Ż(GS,GS) = 0 exactly at all n_max (triangle + parity forces 2l_int odd, impossible). **Calibration exchange constant:** l=1 self-energy at n_max=2 is EXACTLY 1/(4ŽĆ) ŌĆö the S┬▓ Weyl exchange constant. The scalar graph QED is ŽĆ-free (ŌäÜ[ŌłÜ2,ŌłÜ3,ŌłÜ6,...]); the vector photon introduces exactly one transcendental per loop: ŽĆ, through the S┬▓ solid angle normalization. **The selection rule partition (Dirac electrons):** 1 rule from graph topology (always survives) ŌåÆ 6 rules from angular momentum conservation (CG + E1 + triangle, costs exactly 1/(4ŽĆ) per loop) ŌåÆ 1 rule from Dirac spinor phase constraint (zero cost ŌĆö kinematic identity of the vertex). The 7ŌåÆ8 transition does NOT require second-quantized field theory when using Dirac electrons. Calibration: Tr(╬Ż) ├Ś 4ŽĆ = 176/15 (exact rational). Papers 28 and 18 updated. Key files: `geovac/vector_qed.py`, `tests/test_vector_qed.py` (99 tests), `debug/vector_qed_sprint_memo.md`, `debug/furry_dirac_phase_diagnostic.py`, `debug/l1_photon_block_diag.py`, `debug/data/l1_photon_block_diag.json`.
- Bound-state QED arc ŌĆö Lamb shift from scratch (LS-1 ŌåÆ LS-4, May 2026): four-sprint sequence delivering the first bound-state QED observable computed in GeoVac, alongside Paper 34 (Projection Taxonomy and Empirical Matches Catalogue). **(LS-1)** Standard one-loop Lamb shift formula on the Dirac-on-S┬│ infrastructure; ╬öE_VP(2SŌéü/Ōéé) = ŌłÆ27.13 MHz from VP coefficient ╬Ā = 1/(48ŽĆ┬▓) cross-checks the textbook Uehling shift to <1%; total Lamb shift 1025.06 MHz at ŌłÆ3.10% (Bethe logs imported from Drake-Swainson 1990). **(LS-2)** Velocity-form Bethe log via Coulomb Sturmians at exponent ╬╗=Z/n ŌĆö structural identity flagged: **the Sturmian basis at the right exponent IS the GeoVac S┬│ Fock graph re-parameterized for bound-state space**, "Sturmian sum" and "Fock graph sum" are two names for the same object. Result: ln kŌéĆ(2S) = 2.726 (ŌłÆ3.1% vs Drake), ln kŌéĆ(1S) = 2.924 (ŌłÆ2.0%); ln kŌéĆ(2P) divergent (velocity-form J/I ŌåÆ Ōł× for Ōäō>0). **(LS-3)** Acceleration form for s-states reduces truncation by 3.3├Ś: ln kŌéĆ(2S) = 2.786 (ŌłÆ0.92%), ln kŌéĆ(1S) = 3.002 (+0.60%); 2P remains divergent ŌĆö closure ╬Ż_m|Ō¤©2P|p|mŌ¤®|┬▓(E_mŌłÆE_2P) ŌåÆ 0 EXACTLY for Ōäō>0 by Žł_2P(0)=0, structural floor (S-tier in Paper 34 ┬¦V.B). T+A error decomposition demonstrated to machine precision: T(Bethe log) = +3.5 MHz, A(one-loop ╬▒ŌüĄ ceiling) = ŌłÆ32.78 MHz, sum = actual residual. **(LS-4)** Drake-Swainson asymptotic-subtraction regularization implemented as the **13th projection** in Paper 34's Layer 2 dictionary. Splits spectral sum at intermediate K into ╬▓_low(N,K) + ╬▓_high(K) with K-cancellation verified to machine precision over K Ōłł [0.05, 200] (3.6 orders of magnitude). Closes 2P structural floor: ln kŌéĆ(2P) = ŌłÆ0.0307 at N=40 (+2.40% vs Drake), heading to <1% at N=100; **3D Bethe log at N=40 lands at ŌłÆ0.005236 (ŌłÆ0.24% vs Drake ŌłÆ0.005249), the cleanest from-scratch Bethe-log result in the framework**. Combined Lamb shift at N=40 reads 1053.76 MHz (ŌłÆ0.39%) but **agent honestly flagged this as fortuitous T+A cancellation** (T_2S=+28.8 MHz from N=40 truncation in J/I evaluation, A=ŌłÆ32.78 MHz one-loop ceiling); at NŌåÆŌł× residual returns to LS-1 baseline ŌłÆ3.10% set by missing ╬▒ŌüĄ multi-loop. Drake denominator D = 2(2Ōäō+1)ZŌü┤/n┬│ is purely combinatorial-rational (extends s-wave contact density 2ZŌü┤/n┬│ to Ōäō>0 via 2Ōäō+1 angular degeneracy); flagged for review whether this is "empirical determination from convergence" or "standard Drake-Swainson convention." LS-5 future work: derive D from Schwartz integral form. VP-2 found ╬▓(C) = ╬▓(continuum) ŌłÆ ╬▓(graph) verified to machine precision: **the projection constant is a quotient of two power laws, not a single calibration constant** ŌĆö there is no universal C; per-diagram is intrinsic. - **Coupled composition (Track CB, v2.0.37)** ŌĆö NEGATIVE RESULT. Scoping investigation: replace PK with explicit cross-block ERIs in composed architecture. LiH at max_n=2: 854 Pauli terms (2.56├Ś composed 334), 85.69 Ha 1-norm (2.30├Ś composed 37.33), 88 QWC groups (4.19├Ś composed 21). 4-electron FCI: coupled gives 29% error (WORST) vs composed 15%, no-PK-no-cross 10.9%. Root cause: cross-block ERIs add core-valence repulsion but the composed orbital basis (different Z per block) has no cross-center nuclear attraction (h1 terms where orbitals feel the other nucleus). Adding V_ee cross-terms without V_ne cross-terms is energetically unbalanced. Cross-center h1 requires two-center integrals not available in single-center hydrogenic basis. PK is NOT redundant in second quantization for the composed basis. Key files: `geovac/coupled_composition.py`, `tests/test_coupled_composition.py`, `docs/coupled_composition_scoping.md`.

- **Sprint of 2026-05-07 (post-WH1-PROVEN convergent-findings session):** five-track sprint testing forward-looking directions after WH1's GH-convergence keystone closure. **Headline:** four independent findings collectively crystallize the framework's structural-skeleton scope. (a) **Track 3 ŌĆö Bertrand ├Ś Hopf-tower SM gauge truncation.** Under the strict-natural reading "G acts transitively on host manifold," U(1), SU(2), SU(3) are the *complete* set of compact Lie groups admitting Wilson constructions on GeoVac sub-manifolds; SU(4)+, Sp(n), G_2, F_4, exceptionals are RULED OUT (would need S^7, S^9, ... which GeoVac does not produce). **GeoVac is gauge-content-saturated by the SM as a structural upper bound.** The forcing mechanism is Bertrand's theorem (1873, only Coulomb 1/r and harmonic r┬▓ have all bound orbits closed) ├Ś the complex-Hopf S^(2nŌłÆ1) ŌåÆ SU(n) tower truncated at n Ōēż 3. Bertrand is classical mechanics ŌĆö not GeoVac-internal ŌĆö so the forcing is structural-given-Bertrand, not structural-from-GeoVac-axioms. Lower bound (why saturated rather than subset) NOT forced. Memo: `debug/sm_gauge_content_forcing_memo.md`. (b) **Angle 2 ŌĆö Inner-factor Mellin engine + Paper 18 ┬¦IV fourth tier.** Two structural theorems on any Krajewski-class finite spectral triple (verified symbolically on SM lepton sector + full SM A_F = Ōäé ŌŖĢ ŌäŹ ŌŖĢ M_3(Ōäé) + two comparators): (i) **╬Ę-trivialization theorem** ŌĆö chirality grading axiom {╬│_F, D_F} = 0 forces Tr(D_F^k ┬Ę e^{ŌłÆtD_F┬▓}) ŌēĪ 0 for all odd k, so M3 (vertex-parity Hurwitz / Catalan G / Dirichlet-L) is identically zero on any Connes-Chamseddine-compatible inner factor; (ii) **AC factorization theorem** ŌĆö D┬▓ = D_GV┬▓ ŌŖŚ 1 + 1 ŌŖŚ D_F┬▓ because the cross term {D_GV ŌŖŚ 1, ╬│_GV ŌŖŚ D_F} vanishes by outer chirality anticommutation. Combined Mellin output factorizes as (outer M_i ring) ├Ś (inner Yukawa Dirichlet ring); ŽĆ-content sits entirely in outer factor; SM-distinguishing parameters sit entirely in inner factor; rings have no overlap. Paper 18 ┬¦IV gained a sixth named tier ŌĆö **"inner-factor input data"** ŌĆö parameter-tied Yukawa Dirichlet ring ŌäÜ[y_1^{ŌłÆ2s}, ..., y_n^{ŌłÆ2s}], categorically disjoint from intrinsic / calibration / embedding / flow / composition tiers. - **Precision catalogue extension ŌĆö Muonium 1S-2S and Positronium 1S HFS (Track 1 of post-MH multi-track launch, 2026-05-08):** two-observable extension of the multi-focal precision arc to round out the e/╬╝/p mass-hierarchy matrix. **Muonium 1S-2S (eŌü╗ on ╬╝Ōü║):** Mu-MASS Crivelli 2018 measurement $\nu = 2{,}455{,}529{,}002.5(9.9)$ MHz reproduced at **ŌłÆ0.11 ppm** by pure rest-mass rescaling from H experimental ($\nu_H \times m_\text{red}(e\mu)/m_\text{red}(ep) = 2{,}455{,}528{,}721$ MHz), and at **ŌłÆ0.25 ppm** by framework Bohr+SE plus cross-register $V_{eN}$ recoil ($2{,}455{,}528{,}394$ MHz). The ŌłÆ0.11 ppm number is the headline: rest-mass projection theorem (Paper 34 ┬¦III.14) verified at sub-ppm between H and Mu, with the residual cleanly attributable to NLO recoil scaling differential ($m_p/m_\mu = 8.88\times$ between systems). Mu has no QCD nuclear structure (point antimuon ŌåÆ no Zemach, no FNS, no polarizability), making it the cleanest possible test of the framework's QED machinery: only LS-8a-class multi-loop QED inputs are external. Sprint MH-A/B (╬╝H) tested eŌåÆ╬╝ swap at unchanged nucleus; this sprint tests the inverse, ╬╝ŌåÆe swap at unchanged lepton with 8.88├Ś lighter nucleus. Framework-native Bohr-Fermi (spinor + Fermi-contact + Fock + rest-mass projection) captures the magnetic dipole-dipole part exactly: $\nu_F = (1/3) m_e c^2 \alpha^4 / h = 116.79$ GHz (machine-precision match to canonical formula). **The annihilation channel $e^+e^- \to \gamma \to e^+e^-$ contributes the remaining 3/12 of LO ($87.59$ GHz) but is NOT framework-native** ŌĆö virtual-loop second-quantized field-theory effect, not generated by the framework's bare action. Same wall as K├żll├®n-Sabry two-loop VP for muonic H. Framework + Layer-2 annihilation = LO total $204.39$ GHz vs experimental $203.389$ GHz at +0.49% ŌĆö multi-loop QED (Czarnecki-Melnikov-Yelkhovsky 2000, $\alpha^5 m_e c^2/h$) closes the rest. **New finding for the multi-focal architecture:** Roothaan multipole termination at $L_\text{max} = 2 \ell_\text{max}$ is preserved at the equal-mass limit. The termination is a Gaunt selection rule (angular content), not a small-parameter expansion ŌĆö holds independently of $\lambda_a/\lambda_b$ ratio. Multi-focal architecture now verified across the full hierarchy: $\lambda_l \ll \lambda_n$ (H, asymptotic acceleration), $\lambda_l \sim \lambda_n$ (╬╝H, comparable scales), $\lambda_l = \lambda_n$ (Ps, symmetric ŌĆö no acceleration but Gaunt termination preserved). - **Chemistry-solver re-test (Track 2 of post-MH multi-track launch, 2026-05-08):** tests whether the multi-focal Phase C closures (balanced coupled + cross-center V_ne via ShibuyaŌĆōWulfman + screened W1c via `cross_center_screened_vne`) close, persist, or change the v2.0.32 baseline R_eq drift. **Combined verdict: first-row drift PERSISTS at Track CD level (Phase C is no-op for LiH); second-row W1c-residual orthogonality wall EMPIRICALLY CONFIRMED by NaH binding determination.** Architectural finding: the v2.0.32 baseline drift was diagnosed in the level-4 PK-composed PES solver (`composed_diatomic.py`); the Phase C closures live in the qubit-encoded balanced coupled architecture (`balanced_coupled.py`), which is structurally a different solver with no separate `l_max` parameter (basis enumerates at `(n,l,m)` with `l<n`, so `n_max` couples radial + angular). **The chemistry-solver upgrade the framework HAS already received is the balanced-coupled construction itself (Track CD, v2.0.39, April 2026), which reduced the original PK-composed wall (+0.18 bohr/l_max) by 3├Ś to +0.054 bohr/n_max via cross-block ERIs + cross-center V_ne via Shibuya-Wulfman.** That upgrade shipped before Phase C; Phase C did not move it further for first-row. **First-row LiH (n_max=2):** W1c bit-identical at 5├Ś10Ōü╗┬╣Ōü┤ Ha across 5-point PES grid ŌĆö confirms the Phase C-W1c diagnostic claim that `_detect_core_type` returns `None` for Z<11 and the screened path collapses to bare path bit-precisely. n_max=2 reproduces Track CD baseline: R_eq = 3.227 bohr (Track CD: 3.226), R_err = 7.03% (Track CD: 7.0%), E_err = 1.71% (Track CD: 1.8%). n_max=3 single point at R=3.015 stalled in 4-electron FCI eigsh on 740k-determinant sparse matrix beyond fork compute budget; Track CD result (R_eq=3.280, drift +0.054 bohr/n_max) accepted as baseline. **Second-row NaH (n_max=2, Q=20, 2e FCI):** the single highest-value follow-up ŌĆö Phase C D-PES regression confirmed 5.4-6.0├Ś cross-V_ne reduction at NaH equilibrium but reportedly could not determine binding because n_e-projected FCI driver was not yet wired in. `coupled_fci_energy` IS that driver. NaH balanced FCI 7-point R-grid (R Ōłł {2.5, 3.0, 3.5, 4.0, 5.0, 7.0, 10.0}) at max_n=2 ran in 7 seconds total. **Result: PES monotonically descends in BOTH `screened=False` (Sprint 7 baseline) AND `screened=True` (W1c)** ŌĆö no internal minimum at any tested R, R_min sits at the smallest R-grid point in both cases. **W1c reduces edge-to-dissociation gap by 17.5├Ś** (bare: ŌłÆ6.24 Ha; screened: ŌłÆ0.36 Ha), three times more than the 5.4-6├Ś single-R diagnostic, but binding is NOT recovered. **The W1c-residual orthogonality wall named in Phase C is now empirically confirmed at the FCI level**: the H valence orbital Ōåö [Ne]-core orthogonality (Phillips-Kleinman-class) sits beyond the Hartree screening of Z_eff(Žü) that W1c implements. The architectural difference between first-row binding and second-row non-binding is that first-row uses an explicit core block in the FCI sector (electrons resolve their own orthogonality), while second-row uses a frozen-core potential (orthogonality must be enforced externally; W1c does not yet do so). **The W1c-residual orthogonality wall is the single remaining engineering closure for second-row chemistry.** A Phillips-Kleinman-class projection on the H valence orbital against the [Ne] core in cross-center geometry is the mechanical fix. Files: `debug/chemistry_solver_retest_lih.py`, `debug/chemistry_solver_retest_lih_quick_nmax2.py`, `debug/chemistry_solver_retest_lih_nmax3.py`, `debug/chemistry_solver_retest_nah.py`, `debug/data/chemistry_solver_retest_lih.json`, `debug/data/chemistry_solver_retest_nah.json`, `debug/chemistry_solver_retest_lih_memo.md`, `debug/chemistry_solver_retest_synthesis_memo.md`.

- **Phillips-Kleinman cross-center sprint (post-Track-2 chemistry-solver follow-up, 2026-05-08):** named engineering closure for the W1c-residual orthogonality wall. **Verdict: HONEST NEGATIVE ŌĆö PK reduces NaH descent depth from 0.357 Ha (W1c only) to 0.305 Ha at standard absolute-PK parameters ($E_v = 0$), a 14.6% improvement, but does NOT close the wall.** PES still monotonically descending, $R_\text{min}$ still at the smallest tested R (2.5 bohr), no internal equilibrium minimum. The W1c-residual orthogonality wall is structurally deeper than W1b alone. New module `geovac/phillips_kleinman_cross_center.py` (~280 lines, 21 tests passing) implements the standard PK operator-form approximation $\Delta H_{pq}^\text{PK} = \sum_c (E_v - E_c) S_{pc} S_{cq}$ with cross-center overlaps $S_{pc}$ via 2D Gauss-Legendre ├Ś radial-grid quadrature, real-SH azimuthal selection ($m_p^\text{signed} = m_c^\text{signed}$) enforced exactly, Clementi-Roetti HF eigenvalues for [Ne]-core orbitals (Na: $E_{1s} = -40.479$ Ha, $E_{2s} = -2.797$ Ha, $E_{2p} = -1.518$ Ha), direction-based rotation reusing `shibuya_wulfman._build_block_rotation_matrix`. Wired into `geovac/balanced_coupled.py` via `pk_cross_center: bool = False` and `pk_E_valence_ref: float = 0.0` kwargs (bit-exact backward compat when off, verified). 4-config NaH PES at n_max=2: bare 6.244 Ha descent ŌåÆ screened (W1c) 0.357 Ha ŌåÆ screened+PK 0.305 Ha ŌåÆ still 4├Ś deeper than experimental $D_e \approx 0.075$ Ha. Strong-PK probe ($E_v$ scan) shows minimum-depth signature near $E_v = 100$ Ha (descent reduced to 0.148 Ha with hint at internal min) but this is unphysical parameter tuning. **Diagnosis of remaining wall:** candidate sources beyond W1c+W1b PK: (i) inner-core penetration physics (real H 1s tail in unscreened nucleus region), (ii) hydrogenic $Z_\text{orb}=1$ basis on the Na valence side being qualitatively wrong (it is not the actual Na 3s orbital but a generic $Z_\text{eff}=1$ hydrogenic function), (iii) cross-block ERI treatment between Na valence and H valence at mismatched effective charges. Most likely next engineering target: replace the $Z_\text{orb}=1$ basis on the Na center with radial Schr├Čdinger eigenstates of the FrozenCore $Z_\text{eff}(r)$ potential (infrastructure already exists in `neon_core._solve_screened_radial`). Strict Schmidt orthogonalization is the mathematically definitive but expensive alternative. Paper 17 ┬¦6.10 gained "two solvers, two drift signatures" subsection (architectural clarification: drift lives in `composed_diatomic.py`, balanced is `balanced_coupled.py`). Paper 19 gained `\subsection{sec:w1c_residual}` documenting the W1c-residual wall, the PK cross-center engineering closure, the negative result with 4-config descent table, and the next-target diagnosis. - **Sprint Mu Lamb shift (precision catalogue extension, 2026-05-08):** muonium 2SŌéü/Ōéé-2PŌéü/Ōéé Lamb shift completes the e/╬╝/p mass-hierarchy matrix at four operating points. **Framework-native: $1047.63$ MHz vs Karshenboim 2005 theoretical reference $1047.49(5)$ MHz, residual $+0.135$ MHz / $+0.013\%$ ŌĆö the cleanest one-loop QED match in the catalogue at this mass-hierarchy operating point.** Architecture: Paper 36 LS-1..LS-7 transferred verbatim to Mu under rest-mass projection (Paper 34 ┬¦III.14); $\beta = 2/(m_\text{red}\alpha) = 275.40$ vs 274.22 for normal H ŌĆö same contact regime, full Uehling kernel and contact form agree to 0.24 MHz. **Pure rest-mass rescaling cross-check:** Paper 36 H framework value $1052.19 \times m_\text{red}(e\mu)/m_\text{red}(ep) = 1047.696$ MHz vs native compute $1047.625$ MHz ŌĆö agreement to 0.071 MHz / 7 ppm, sharpest verification yet of the rest-mass projection theorem at the Lamb-shift bracket level. **Recoil-absorption observation:** the framework's pure Eides ┬¦3.2 SE bracket gives $+1074.13$ MHz; Karshenboim's "SE one-loop" itemization is $+1085.84$ MHz, separately-itemizing "Recoil NLO $-11.30$ MHz". The two differ by $\sim 0.4$ MHz ŌĆö the framework's $m_\text{red}$ rescaling absorbs Karshenboim's itemized recoil at the bracket level, so naively adding the recoil to the framework total double-counts. **Why Mu Lamb shift is the cleanest of the four mass-hierarchy points:** (i) no FNS ($\mu^+$ point lepton), (ii) no QCD polarizability, (iii) Uehling regime in contact-form sweet spot, (iv) $m_\text{red} \approx 1$ keeps Eides bracket at calibration point, (v) recoil mixing absorbed into rescaling. The single Layer-2 multi-loop input (Karshenboim $\alpha^2(Z\alpha)^4$ at $+0.20$ MHz) is within the $+0.13$ MHz native residual ŌĆö **the framework's one-loop QED is sufficient to reproduce Mu Lamb shift theory at sub-$0.05\%$ in this regime**. Mass-hierarchy comparison: H Lamb $-0.534\%$ (m_redŌēł1, m_nŌēł1836); ╬╝H Lamb $-0.92\%$ native / $-0.10\%$ +lit (m_redŌēł186, m_nŌēł1836); Mu 1S-2S $-0.11$ ppm (rest-mass rescaling); Mu Lamb $+0.013\%$ native (m_redŌēł1, m_nŌēł207). - **Sprint CP┬▓ packing scoping (Track 3 of post-MH multi-track launch, 2026-05-08):** scoping pass on whether the Paper 0 packing axiom admits a faithful analog on natural compact homogeneous spaces beyond S┬│ ŌĆö primary focus CP┬▓ = SU(3)/U(2) and the SU(3) (p,q) irrep lattice; secondary 5%-passes on SŌüČ = GŌéé/SU(3), HP┬╣ = SŌü┤, CP┬│ = SU(4)/U(3), full flag SU(3)/T, OP┬▓ = FŌéä/Spin(9), Grassmannians. **Verdict: PARTIAL CLOSURE ŌĆö does NOT land in the strong sense.** (a) The SU(3) (p,q) irrep lattice closes mathematically as a hexagonal-connectivity graph: 15 lattice points through level k=4, dim(p,q) = (p+1)(q+1)(p+q+2)/2, Casimir CŌéé(p,q) = (p┬▓+q┬▓+pq)/3 + (p+q), 6-neighbor adjacency from (1,0) ŌŖŚ (p,q) = (p+1,q) ŌŖĢ (pŌłÆ1,q+1) ŌŖĢ (p,qŌłÆ1) and (0,1)-tensor ŌĆö the triangular lattice the PI's QCD intuition pointed at. Cumulative state count ╬Ż_{p+q=K} dim(p,q) = (K+1)(K+2)┬▓(K+3)/12 (closed form, verified through K=4 by direct sum: 1, 6, 20, 50, 105). (b) CP┬▓ hosts the (p,p)-symmetric sub-lattice with LaplaceŌĆōBeltrami spectrum ╬╗_p = p(p+2) and multiplicities (p+1)┬│ (vs S┬│'s (p+1)┬▓ at the same eigenvalue ŌĆö extra (p+1) factor is the Hopf-fibration U(1) direction). (c) **Neither closes from a packing-axiom motivation with the same epistemic standing as Paper 0.** Paper 0's axioms ("binary distinguishability + 2D isotropy") are **rank-1 specific**; they do not lift to rank 2 without becoming representation-theoretic. The "minimum to define a metric" argument has no SU(3) analog; the "isotropy ŌåÆ uniform density" axiom has no rank-2 analog (only SU(3)-equivariance, which is rep-theoretic input not packing-axiom input). The scaling rule (irrep dim formula) comes from Weyl's character formula, not annular-area counting. (d) **Coulomb/HO category obstruction confirmed at every higher-rank candidate:** Paper 24 ┬¦V four-layer asymmetry (spectrum-computing L_0; calibration ŽĆ; Wilson-with-matter; combinatorial vocabulary) ŌĆö CP┬▓/(p,q) lattice sit at "layer-iv only" (combinatorial vocabulary without dynamics structure), structurally distinct from S┬│ (layers iŌĆōiv) and SŌüĄ Hardy (layer iii partial). Calibration ŽĆ (╬║ = ŌłÆ1/16, K = ŽĆ(B+FŌłÆ╬ö)) is S┬│-specific by Paper 23 ┬¦IV Fock rigidity theorem; does not transfer. (e) Eightfold-way correspondence (octet at (1,1) dim 8, decuplet at (3,0) dim 10, 27 at (2,2) dim 27) is **tautological**, not predictive ŌĆö the (p,q) lattice contains the eightfold way *because* it is SU(3) rep theory by construction. (f) **Recommendation: do not prioritize CP┬▓ as the next major track.** Continue with Tracks 1 (multi-focal precision catalogue) and 2 (chemistry solver re-test). The (p,q) lattice and CP┬▓ spherical-rep tower remain available as secondary catalogue-style tools for organizing SU(3)-related observations within the existing framework. (g) **One non-tautological open question flagged:** the extra (p+1) Hopf-direction multiplicity on CP┬▓ could in principle host U(1) hypercharge ├Ś SU(3) color structure at the kinematic level if the U(1) direction has dynamical content ŌĆö opportunistic 1-2 week sub-sprint scoped in ┬¦5.1 of memo. **Honest synthesis:** the "second packing axiom" question (W3 in CLAUDE.md ┬¦1.7 multi-focal-wall taxonomy) is **structurally distinct** from "find a packing on a different geometry" ŌĆö whatever generates inner-factor calibration data does NOT need to be a packing-axiom analog on a higher-rank geometry, and this scoping does not move the W3 question. - **Precision catalogue extension ŌĆö Muonium 1S HFS (post-Phillips-Kleinman, 2026-05-08):** closes the muonium catalogue triple (1S-2S, 2S-2P Lamb, 1S HFS) by extending the framework's Bohr-Fermi machinery to the leptonic-nucleus regime. **Framework-native: BF Dirac ├Ś $(1+a_e)(1+a_\mu)$ Schwinger $= 4464.1905$ MHz vs Liu 1999 $4463.302765(53)$ MHz, residual $+0.8877$ MHz / $+199$ ppm.** Outside the sub-100 ppm bears-fruit threshold but **the cleanest LS-8a multi-loop isolation in the catalogue**: leptonic point-nucleus (antimuon) means residual is purely $\alpha^2(Z\alpha)$ multi-loop QED + cross-register recoil NLO + hadronic VP ŌĆö no QCD nuclear-structure budget interfering (no Zemach, no polarizability, no FNS). The +199 ppm is therefore the empirical depth of the LS-8a wall at $\alpha^2(Z\alpha)$ for Bohr-Fermi-class observables in clean isolation; the wall sits below leading-order precision in this regime (i.e., one-loop QED almost gets us there, with the structural overshoot from the doubled $(1+a_e)(1+a_\mu)$ Schwinger pattern unique to leptonic-nucleus systems). - **Precision catalogue extension ŌĆö Deuterium 1S HFS (post-MH continuation, 2026-05-08):** extends the multi-focal precision arc to the I=1 nuclear-spin axis, complementing Sprint MH (e/╬╝ swap at unchanged proton) and Track 1 Mu/Ps (╬╝/p swap at unchanged electron, equal-mass limit) by varying nuclear spin with everything else held fixed. **Bohr-Fermi strict prediction lands at +40 ppm** vs Wineland-Ramsey 1972 $\nu_\text{HFS}(D, 1S) = 327.384352522(2)$ MHz ŌĆö the cleanest framework-native verification of the I=1 cross-register angular coupling structure in the catalogue. **Convention key (the only subtle point):** the atomic-physics Hamiltonian convention uses $g_N = 2 \mu_N/\mu_N^\text{unit}$ independent of I (matches CODATA $g_p = 5.586$ for proton at $2I=1$), giving $g_d^\text{atomic} = 2 \times 0.857 = 1.715$ (differs from CODATA's $g_d = 0.857$ by the factor $2I = 2$). The (2I+1)/2 = 3/2 multiplicity factor between F=3/2 and F=1/2 levels is Clebsch-Gordan, NOT a new mechanism. **Multi-focal architecture verdict at I=1: leading_order_I_independent.** The Fermi-contact Hamiltonian $A_\text{hf} \hat{I} \cdot \hat{S} \delta^3(r)$ is operator-identical for I=1/2 and I=1; Roothaan multipole termination at $L_\text{max} = 2 \ell_\text{max}$ is angular content, not nuclear-spin content. The deuteron's nonzero electric quadrupole moment $Q_d = 0.286$ efm┬▓ couples only to gradients (negligible for s-states). **Framework-native chain:** BF strict (327.40 MHz, +40 ppm) ŌåÆ BF + recoil (327.13, -777 ppm) ŌåÆ +Schwinger $a_e$ (327.51, +384 ppm) ŌåÆ +leading Zemach with $r_Z(D) = 2.593$ fm Friar-Payne 2005 (327.48, **+286 ppm**). Operator-level Zemach via `geovac.magnetization_density.hydrogen_zemach_eides_leading_order` matches analytic $-2 Z m_e r_Z$ Eides leading-order to $10^{-14}$ ppm; profile (Gaussian vs exponential) independence preserved. Cumulative residual +286 ppm sits inside the budgeted **W2a + W3 walls**: deuteron polarizability ~+44 ppm (Pachucki-Yerokhin 2010, QCD-internal NN dynamics ŌĆö W3 inner-factor calibration), multi-loop QED ~few ppm (LS-8a wall), recoil NLO + finite-size charge ~few ppm (Layer-2 input). **Coverage matrix completes:** the e/╬╝/p mass-hierarchy axis (lepton mass, nuclear mass, equal-mass) AND the I=1/2 vs I=1 nuclear-spin axis are both now empirically verified at sub-100 ppm on framework-native parts across six precision systems (H 21cm, ╬╝H Lamb, ╬╝H HFS, Mu 1S-2S, Ps HFS, D 1S HFS). - **Cleanup sprint ŌĆö production-code side findings closed (2026-05-08, post-catalogue):** two parallel cleanup tracks closed both side findings the He 2┬╣S-2┬│S sprint surfaced. **(T1 `hypergeometric_slater.compute_rk_float` bug ŌĆö diagnosis wider than initially flagged.)** The "n Ōēź 12 broken" symptom was the visible failure mode of a pervasive float-path issue: catastrophic cancellation between O(10┬▓ŌüĄ) Laguerre-product terms summing to O(10┬╣┬╣) silently degraded accuracy starting at n = 6 (rel err 1e-7 at n=6, 1e-4 at n=8, 0.2 at n=10, fully wrong sign at n Ōēź 12). The k Ōēź 2 ssss crash was a separate Gaunt-violation issue (negative power in incomplete-gamma kernel for k > l_a + l_b ŌĆö physically forbidden but no clean error path). Fix: threshold dispatch at n = 4 ŌĆö n Ōēż 4 uses the existing fast pure-float path bit-identically (~240 ╬╝s/call, no regression), n Ōēź 5 delegates to `compute_rk_algebraic` and casts to float at the end (correct at any n; n=8: 0.54 s uncached, n=12: 6.5 s, n=20: ~1 min, all paid once per unique quartet via existing `_CACHE_FLOAT`). Gaunt-violating quartets now raise informative `ValueError`. 38 new regression tests in `tests/test_hypergeometric_slater.py` cover n=6..20 across ssss/pppp/spsp/mixed quartets, all verified against `compute_rk_exact` ground truth. **Quantitative refresh resolved (2026-05-08 same-day continuation):** the He 2┬╣S-2┬│S sprint was re-run from scratch with the fixed evaluator (full n_max=2..11 sweep, ~30 min wall time, n_max=11 alone 988s `t_build`). **Trajectory is bit-identical to the original at displayed 0.1 cmŌü╗┬╣ precision**; largest shift across all n_max is **0.05 cmŌü╗┬╣**, two orders of magnitude smaller than the cleanup-sprint worst-case estimate of 10-30 cmŌü╗┬╣ and four orders of magnitude smaller than the +762 cmŌü╗┬╣ structural residual. The +11.863% verdict at n_max=11 stands; Paper 34 ┬¦V.B row gained an annotation but kept the +11.86% number unchanged. **Why the bug had minimal numerical impact on this observable:** the catastrophic-cancellation regime hits *same-shell large-n* integrals hardest, while the He 2┬╣S-2┬│S splitting is dominated by exchange integrals K(1s, ns) with at least one small-n index where the cancellation regime is much milder. Additionally, numerical noise in the integrals is *correlated* between singlet and triplet sectors (same orbital configurations, different spin coupling) and partially cancels in the splitting itself. Absolute energies E(2┬│S) and E(2┬╣S) (both ~2.7% error) are slightly more sensitive to high-n noise than the splitting (11.9% error), but the dominant residual in all three is the ╬║-induced excited-state non-variationality, not integral precision. Variational violation, anti-cancellation, structural finding all preserved. Memo ┬¦3.1 added documenting the refresh; JSON regenerated; log at `debug/data/he_refresh.log`. **Net cleanup: both side findings (T1 and T2) are closed and the quantitative refresh confirms the catalogue conclusion stands.** **(T2 `casimir_ci.compute_he_spectrum` state-labeling ŌĆö promoted ss-only sub-block from sprint workaround to production API.)** New kwarg `subblock: Optional[Tuple[int, int]] = None` on both `build_graph_native_fci` and `compute_he_spectrum`; default `None` preserves existing behavior bit-identically (verified by 4 backward-compat regression tests at n_max=2,3,4); `subblock=(0,0)` gives clean ┬╣S/┬│S, `(0,1)` gives ┬╣P/┬│P, etc. Order-invariant (sorting before comparison). Docstrings updated to document the M_L-mixing problem at n_max Ōēź 3 and recommend the right kwarg. 24 new tests in `tests/test_casimir_ci.py` cover backward-compat, ss-only at n_max=3,4,5 (reproduces sprint memo ┬¦3 reference at n_max=5: 7308.7713 cmŌü╗┬╣, matching to 0.01 cmŌü╗┬╣), sp sub-block, edge cases (negative-l raises ValueError, empty shells, Hermiticity, Hund ordering). All 21 production call sites verified backward-compatible ŌĆö no caller updates needed. **Net status:** both side findings closed; combined test verification 122/122 pass + 9 slow skipped (`pytest tests/test_hypergeometric_slater.py tests/test_casimir_ci.py -x`). - **W1c-residual NaH closure attempt (Track 3 of 2026-05-09 post-multi-track sprint, HONEST NEGATIVE on binding + DIAGNOSTIC POSITIVE):** Engineering closure for the W1c-residual orthogonality wall named in the post-Track-2 chemistry-solver re-test (PK cross-center synthesis memo ┬¦7 recommendation #1). Replaces the hydrogenic Z_orb=1 Na valence h1 diagonal with the actual Schr├Čdinger eigenvalue of the FrozenCore Z_eff(r) potential. New module `geovac/screened_valence_basis.py` (~280 lines, 25 fast tests passing) provides `screened_valence_eigenvalue(Z_nuc, block_n, l, n_val_offset)` and `apply_screened_valence_correction()`. Wired into `build_balanced_hamiltonian` via `screened_valence_basis: bool = False` kwarg with bit-exact backward compat preserved (LiH 878 Pauli regression bit-identical at machine precision). **Eigenvalue substitution verified to literature**: Na 3s = -0.170 Ha (CR67 single-zeta), Na 4s = -0.067 Ha, Na 4p = -0.051 Ha ŌĆö all physically bound, sign and magnitude consistent with Clementi-Roetti HF tabulation. h1 diagonal correction is a +0.611 Ha trace shift on the NaH valence (3s + 4s + 3┬Ę4p), large compared to descent depth (0.357 Ha after W1c). **8-configuration NaH PES at max_n=2 (Q=20, 2e FCI)**: all 8 still monotonically descending, NO internal equilibrium minimum. R_min = 2.5 (smallest tested) for every config. Descent-depth ladder: bare 6.244 ŌåÆ +W1c 0.357 (17.5├Ś) ŌåÆ +W1c+PK 0.305 (1.17├Ś addl) ŌåÆ +W1c+PK+SV 0.313 (0.97├Ś addl, slight worsening). The screened-valence diagonal correction does NOT close the wall. **Critical structural finding (the substantive result)**: the SV correction is **R-independent at the diagonal h1 level** ŌĆö eigenvalues are properties of the on-center potential, not of the bond. The screened correction matrix is bit-identical at R=2.5 and R=10 (max abs diff 5.55├Ś10Ōü╗┬╣ŌüĘ). A constant diagonal h1 shift cannot affect the descent-depth (an R-dependent energy difference). The named target ("replace Z_orb=1 hydrogenic Na valence basis with screened Schr├Čdinger eigenstates") is **incomplete as named** ŌĆö it requires wavefunction-shape substitution in cross-V_ne and within-block ERIs, not just diagonal h1 substitution. **Diagnostic experiment (debug/w1c_residual_nah_track3_diag.py)**: testing the cross-V_ne integral with hydrogenic-shape labels at the *physical* n (block_n=1, l=0 ŌåÆ n_phys=3 hydrogenic 3s instead of 1s) shows that the framework over-attracts by 0.81 Ha at R=2.5 vs the physical-n shape, and by only 0.14 Ha at R=10. **Differential -0.674 Ha** ŌĆö about **1.9├Ś larger than the W1c-residual descent (0.357 Ha)**. Structural reading: a wavefunction-shape substitution would over-correct from the current attraction profile and **likely produce a binding minimum**. The genuine residual lives in cross-V_ne integration shape, not diagonal eigenvalue. The hydrogenic Z=1 1s on Na has mean radius 1.50 bohr; the actual Na 3s screened wavefunction has mean radius 4.47 bohr ŌĆö opposite shape biases at the orbital extent level. **Verdict**: the SV diagonal correction is necessary architectural infrastructure (wired and tested) but not sufficient for binding. Next named engineering closure is **wavefunction-shape substitution in cross-center V_ne and within-block ERIs**, not strict-Schmidt orthogonalization. Strict-Schmidt remains the mathematically definitive but expensive alternative; the diagnostic suggests the cheaper "physical-n hydrogenic relabeling" of the Na valence states would close most of the wall and is a 1-week sprint, not multi-week. **Pattern crystallization**: the diagnostic-before-engineering rule (memory `feedback_diagnostic_before_engineering.md`, 2026-05-08) applies inside this sprint. Two engineering attempts (PK cross-center + screened-valence diagonal) have now landed clean modules but failed to close binding; the third pre-implementation diagnostic (cross-V_ne shape sweep) shows the genuine target is in cross-V_ne shape, not diagonal h1. Combined with G4-1's $K_{S^2}(t) \sim 2 r_h^2/t$ gives $I_E^{\rm conical}(\alpha) = (r_h^2 \Lambda^2/6)(1/\alpha - \alpha)$. Factor-of-2 calibration with G7's $G_{\rm eff} = 6\pi/\Lambda^2$ from scalar vs Dirac conical-defect coefficient (standard CC literature). - **Discrete-for-skeleton standing rule (2026-05-26, v3.3.2):** PI flagged a recurrent anti-pattern:\ defaulting to `mpmath` high-dps + PSLQ + increasing-N_max sweeps when computing Layer 1 (skeleton) quantities that have exact discrete answers via `sympy` `Rational` arithmetic, exact symbolic diagonalization, or closed-form recursions. The pattern is a continuum-physics habit (continuum observables are usually transcendental, PSLQ-on-floats is the right tool there) imported wrongly to the skeleton regime, where every Layer 1 quantity is exact at every n_max by construction. Wastes compute and hides structure behind numerical noise. New standing rule `feedback_discrete_for_skeleton.md` added to canonical memory; MEMORY.md index updated with cross-reference from existing `feedback_algebraic_first` (this rule is the skeleton-specific sharpening). PSLQ remains valid as *post-discrete* identification on Layer 2 quantities (the AdS-S^7 sweep was the right tool because the question was Layer 2 ring identification on a value already derived via Hurwitz). Diagnostic in the rule body:\ Layer 1 / Layer 2 indicators + the right pattern (compute exactly first, PSLQ only for ring identification) + edge case (PSLQ as Layer-assignment diagnostic at modest precision is valid). No production code modified.

Framework's first operator-system-level literal identification of a Lorentzian QFT theorem at finite cutoff. **Honest scope:** closure at finite n_max and finite N_t, NOT continuum / GH-limit / Lorentzian-propinquity limit. No published Lorentzian propinquity construction exists as of May 2026 (Latr├®moli├©re 2017/2026, Hekkelman-McDonald 2024 a/b, Toyota 2023, Farsi-Latr├®moli├©re 2024/2025 all strictly Riemannian). Constructing Lorentzian propinquity is named Sprint L3 (6-12 months original NCG mathematics). Uses Sprint L2-D resolution R1 (truthful Camporesi-Higuchi D_GV; the BBB universal axiom ŽćD = -DŽć failure on D_GV is preserved scope finding from L2-D but does NOT obstruct L2-E because the wedge construction is K_L^{╬▒,W}-driven, not D_L-driven). **WH1 PROVEN is NOT re-opened.** Files: `geovac/modular_hamiltonian_lorentzian.py` (~860 lines), `tests/test_modular_hamiltonian_lorentzian.py` (74 fast + 3 slow tests, all pass; zero regression in 355 upstream baseline tests across L1 + L2-B + L2-C + L2-D), `debug/l2_e_modular_hamiltonian_lorentzian_compute.py`, `debug/data/l2_e_modular_hamiltonian_lorentzian.json`, `debug/l2_e_modular_hamiltonian_lorentzian_memo.md` (~5000 words). Paper edits: Paper 32 ┬¦VIII.E.E new subsection `sec:l2e_krein_modular_hamiltonian` (~200 lines); Paper 42 ┬¦11 new "Lorentzian closure at finite cutoff" section (~250 lines, with ┬¦10 O3 refinement); Paper 34 ┬¦V.E L2-E closure paragraph + ┬¦III.27 status flip to "literal identification at Krein level (finite cutoff)"; Paper 31 ┬¦8 empirical-verification subsection.

- **Sprint L2-F.1 + Pythagorean extension scoping (2026-05-17):** Two-track post-L2-closure sprint testing whether the Paper 42 ┬¦7.2 H_local ŌēĀ D_W structural finding has additional algebraic structure beyond the bit-exact residual values reported by L2-E. **Headline structural result:** on the hemispheric wedge $W_L$ of the Lorentzian Krein space, $\langle H_{\mathrm{local}}, D_W^L \rangle_{\mathrm{HS}} = 0$ **bit-exact at every panel cell tested** (n_max Ōłł {1,ŌĆ”,6}, all six witnesses, N_t Ōłł {1, 11}), with closed-form HilbertŌĆōSchmidt squared distance $r^2(n; \kappa_g) = \kappa_g^2 \cdot S(n)/(4\pi^2) + D(n)$ where $S(n) = n(n+1)(n+2)(2n^2+4n-1)/15$ and $D(n) = n(n+1)(n+2)(2n+1)(2n+3)/20$. The $1/\pi^2$ prefactor on $\|H_{\mathrm{local}}\|^2$ is the **master Mellin engine M1 Hopf-base-measure signature** (same $1/\pi^2$ as the L2 quantitative rate $4/\pi$ and as the StefanŌĆōBoltzmann Matsubara prefactor). PSLQ-verified at 100 dps with coefficient ceiling $10^6$. **Mechanism (subspace decomposition, structural sketch):** $H_{\mathrm{local}} = K_\alpha^W/\beta = J_{\mathrm{polar}}/(2\pi)$ lives in the diagonal subspace of $B(\mathcal{K}_W)$ (in the full-Dirac basis under the BW choice); $D_W^L$ lives in the off-diagonal subspace ($\Delta n = \pm 1$, intertwines $\pm m_j$ chirality partners). Diagonal and off-diagonal operator subspaces are orthogonal under the HilbertŌĆōSchmidt inner product. The Pythagorean relation $r^2 = \|H_{\mathrm{local}}\|^2 + \|D_W^L\|^2$ is then forced. Formal proof of the subspace decomposition (as opposed to PSLQ-verified empirical observation) is the named follow-on. **Track 1 (six-witness universality):** HS-orthogonality verified universal across all six modular witnesses (BW + HH├Ś2 + Sewell + Unruh├Ś2) at 18 panel cells, max $|\langle H, D\rangle| = 8.9 \times 10^{-16}$. Universality is a $\kappa_g$-linearity corollary of the BW result; the closed form above generalises by $\kappa_g$-substitution. Pythagoras $r^2 = \|H\|^2 + \|D\|^2$ verified at every cell. N_t > 1 spot check at (n_max, N_t) = (3, 11) confirms orthogonality persists in the temporal-derivative regime where $D_L = i(\gamma^0 \otimes \partial_t + D_{\mathrm{GV}} \otimes I)$ adds content beyond $D_{\mathrm{GV}}$. **Track 2 (Pythagorean extension scoping):** two candidate extensions of the orthogonality structure beyond Paper 42/43 spectral triples were scoped diagnostically. (a) **SU(2) Wilson lattice gauge on $S^3$** (Paper 30): **GO-WITH-PREREQS.** Trivial-vacuum orthogonality is automatic (the L_1 = B^T B kinetic term lives in a structurally distinct sector from any candidate "local Hamiltonian" on the lattice gauge sector); needs matter-coupling wired into `geovac/su2_wilson_gauge.py` (~1ŌĆō2 weeks) before the substantive question (survival under Haar averaging at non-trivial $\beta_{\mathrm{Wilson}}$) can be asked. (b) **SU(3) Wilson on $S^5$ Bargmann lattice** (Sprint ST-SU3): **NO-GO**, with four structural obstructions: (i) no spinor sector on the $(N, 0)$ Hardy tower (Paper 24 ┬¦III); (ii) no second-order/first-order distinction with separate Dirac (Paper 24 Theorem 3, HO rigidity); (iii) no half-integer wedge ŌĆö $m_l$ is integer on Bargmann, so the natural modular period is $\pi$ not $2\pi$ and the K spectrum cannot have integer eigenvalues two_m_j; (iv) Coulomb/HO category mismatch resurfaces at the modular-Hamiltonian level ŌĆö same blocker as G4b cross-manifold (`debug/g4_cross_manifold_scoping_memo.md`) and as Sprint L2 ┬¦7.2-class generator distinctions. This establishes the **fourth layer** of the Paper 24 ┬¦V Coulomb/HO asymmetry: (i) spectrum-computing role of $L_0$; (ii) calibration $\pi$; (iii) non-abelian Wilson gauge with natural matter coupling; (iv) **modular-Hamiltonian structure of the wedge KMS state** (the Coulomb side admits HS-orthogonality on the Krein wedge with closed-form M1 prefactor; the HO side does not admit the construction at all). **Paper edits applied (5 edits across 4 papers, all three-pass clean):** Paper 43 ┬¦10.2 new `subsec:pythagorean_orthogonality` with Corollary `cor:pythagorean_orthogonality` (closed form + structural reading + scope statement on formal-proof follow-on); ┬¦11 (Open questions) O4 extended with formal subspace-decomposition proof as named follow-on. Paper 42 ┬¦8 new `rem:pythagorean_underlies_collapse` placing the six-witness collapse inside the HS-orthogonality structure; ┬¦10 O3 extended with Pythagorean refinement (residual norms ŌĆ¢H_local ŌłÆ D_WŌĆ¢_F now have closed-form components, sharpening the open question). Paper 32 ┬¦VIII new `rem:pythagorean_m1_closure` connecting the orthogonality $1/\pi^2$ prefactor to the master Mellin engine M1 closure. Paper 24 ┬¦V new `subsec:asymmetry_layer4` extending the Coulomb/HO asymmetry from three layers to four (Paper 31 ┬¦sec:coulomb_ho cross-reference added). Paper 32 ┬¦VIII.C G4b paragraph revised ŌĆö no longer "fourth layer" since Paper 24 ┬¦V now records four layers explicitly; G4b reframed as sibling of the asymmetry-layer-4 obstruction at the cross-manifold setting. Paper 24 had a pre-existing `\newtheorem{theorem}` and `\newtheorem{corollary}` missing-declaration LaTeX bug (caught + fixed in this session with single-line preamble addition between `\usepackage{xcolor}` and `\begin{document}`); no other Paper 24 content changed. Compilation: Papers 42/43/32 three-pass clean zero substantive warnings; Paper 24 three-pass clean after preamble fix. **Honest scope:** orthogonality is **empirically PSLQ-verified at 18 panel cells** with closed-form $r^2$ matching to coefficient ceiling $10^6$; the **subspace-decomposition mechanism is a structural sketch** sufficient to identify the M1 signature and the diagonal/off-diagonal partition; **formal proof of the subspace decomposition** (operator-theoretic, not panel-PSLQ) is the named follow-on (Option 2 from PI's earlier triage). WH1 PROVEN is not re-opened; this sprint refines L2-E's H_local ŌēĀ D_W finding with additional algebraic structure but does not change the Paper 42 ┬¦10 O3 open-question status. The fourth Coulomb/HO asymmetry layer is genuinely new structural content; Paper 31 ┬¦sec:coulomb_ho three-layer count is now formally extended to four with explicit citation to this sprint. **Bit-exactness rule of thumb (PI-adopted heuristic, recorded as feedback memory):** "bit-exact closure = green light (we're operating on the skeleton); residuals = caution light (Layer 2 work); neither = drift detector needed." The rule organises sprint triage: bit-exact closures (six-witness collapse, Žā_{2ŽĆ}=1, J┬▓=┬▒I, HS-orthogonality) are skeleton operations and warrant publication-grade follow-through; residuals at machine-precision-but-not-zero (e.g. L1 Žā_{2ŽĆ} residual scaling as O(ŌłÜdim_H ┬Ę ╬Ą_machine)) live at the Layer-2 boundary; results that are neither bit-exact nor machine-precision-bounded warrant a drift-detector diagnostic before further engineering. Used productively across L2-F.1, the six-witness probe, and the SU(2)/SU(3) scoping sprints.
