- **Sprint L3b-2 + Paper 45 ŌĆö KŌü║-restricted weak-form Lorentzian propinquity convergence theorem (2026-05-18):** **CLOSED ŌĆö main theorem proved in four sub-sprints on the L3b foundation laid down in v2.46.0.** Single-day sprint closing the convergence-theorem leg of the Lorentzian-extension program for truncated GeoVac spectral triples. To our knowledge the **first published Lorentzian propinquity convergence theorem on truncated Krein spectral triples in the math.OA literature**; concurrent-work audit run during pre-submission hardening returned CLEAR. **Main theorem:** on truncated SU(2) ├Ś U(1)_T Krein spectral triples with $\Krein_{\nmax, \Nt} = \HGV^{\nmax} \otimes \C^{\Nt}$, $\JL = \JL^{\spat} \otimes I_{\Nt}$ at BBB $(m, n) = (4, 6)$ Peskin-Schroeder chiral basis, $\DL = i(\gamma^{0} \otimes \partial_{t} + \DGV \otimes I_{\Nt})$ per van den Dungen 2016 Proposition 4.1, $\Lprop(\Tcal^{L}_{\nmax,\Nt,T}, \Tcal^{L}_{\Manifold}) \le C_{3}^{\mathrm{joint}} \cdot \gamma^{\mathrm{joint}}_{\nmax, \Nt, T} \to 0$ where $\Lprop$ is the **KŌü║-restricted weak-form Lorentzian propinquity** $\Lprop(\Tcal_{1}^{L}, \Tcal_{2}^{L}) := \Lambda(\Tcal_{1}^{+}, \Tcal_{2}^{+})$ on the Krein-positive Hilbert-space restriction $\Kplus = \{|\psi\rangle : \JL|\psi\rangle = +|\psi\rangle\}$ where the Krein product reduces to a positive-definite Hilbert inner product and Latr├®moli├©re 2017/2023 machinery applies verbatim, $C_{3}^{\mathrm{joint}} \le 1$ asymptotically tight (inherited from Paper 38 L3 via the joint Lichnerowicz structural identity), and $\gamma^{\mathrm{joint}}_{\nmax, \Nt, T} = O(\log\nmax/\nmax + T/\Nt)$. **Five-lemma proof transferred from Paper 38 across four sub-sprints.** **(Sub-sprint A ŌĆö joint Lichnerowicz / L3, PROVED.)** Structural identity $[\DL, a_{s} \otimes a_{t}] = i[\DGV, a_{s}] \otimes a_{t}$ ŌĆö the time-chirality cross term $\{\gamma^{0}, \DGV\} = 0$ on the chirality-doubled basis (since $\gamma^{0}$ anticommutes with $\DGV$ as a Cl(3, 1) gamma matrix and $\DGV$ is chirality-diagonal), so the temporal direction contributes **nothing** to the joint commutator and the joint $C_{3}^{\mathrm{joint}} = C_{3}^{\SU(2)}$ verbatim ŌĆö an unexpected structural simplification. **(Sub-sprint B ŌĆö joint cb-norm / L2, PROVED.)** Joint central spectral Fej├®r kernel $\Kjoint = \KSU_{\nmax} \otimes \KU_{\Nt, T}$ on $\SU(2) \times \Uone$ with factorised Plancherel symbol; Bo┼╝ejko-Fendler central-multiplier equality on the amenable compact group product gives joint cb-norm $\cbnorm{S_{\Kjoint}} = 2/(\nmax + 1)$ ŌĆö **$\Nt$-independent**, a second unexpected simplification reflecting the trivial Plancherel structure of $\Uone$. Factorisation exact in sympy rationals. **(Sub-sprint C ŌĆö joint Berezin reconstruction / L4, PROVED.)** Tensor-product Berezin map $\Bjoint = B^{\SU(2)} \otimes B^{\Uone}$ inherits the four required properties (positivity, contractivity, approximate identity with rate $\gamma^{\mathrm{joint}} = O(\log\nmax/\nmax + T/\Nt)$, L3 compatibility) factor-by-factor; PURE_TENSOR structure means no cross-factor verification needed. **(Sub-sprint D ŌĆö KŌü║-weak-form propinquity / L5, PROVED-WITH-NAMED-GAP.)** Latr├®moli├©re tunneling pair $(\Bjoint, \Pjoint)$ assembled on the KŌü║ Hilbert-space restriction; reach and height contributions bounded factor-wise; main theorem follows. **Named gap:** Latr├®moli├©re 2017 ┬¦5 KŌü║-preservation bookkeeping is sketched analytically but not closed in full detail ŌĆö given the trivial-multiplier KŌü║-preservation already established at L3a-1 (Paper 44, v2.46.0), this is bookkeeping rather than an analytical obstruction. **Numerical verification panel:** $\Lprop$ values at $(\nmax, \Nt) \in \{(2, 3), (3, 5), (4, 7)\} = \{2.0746, 1.6101, 1.3223\}$, bit-identical to Paper 38/39's Riemannian SU(2) bound at matching $\nmax$; convergence ratio $\Lprop(4, 7) / \Lprop(2, 3) = 0.6374$ matches Paper 38/39 bit-exactly. Temporal direction expands the multiplier algebra (admissible $a_t$ grows with $\Nt$) but does not tighten the Lipschitz-height bound ŌĆö $\Nt$-dependence lives in reach (╬│-moment), not height (cb-norm), per Sub-sprint B's $\Nt$-independent cb-norm. **Riemannian-limit recovery at $\Nt = 1$ bit-exact** ŌĆö joint construction reduces to Paper 38's single-factor bound bit-exactly because $\Bjoint|_{\Nt = 1} = B^{\SU(2)} \otimes B^{\Uone}_{1, T} = B^{\SU(2)}$ (the $\Nt = 1$ temporal Berezin map is identity on the single Fourier mode). **Paper 45 drafted and pre-submission hardened to ARXIV_READY status:** seventh math.OA standalone in the GeoVac series (siblings 38, 39, 40, 42, 43, 44) at `papers/group1_operator_algebras/paper_45_lorentzian_propinquity.tex` (1,721 lines, 8,088 words, 18 pages, three-pass clean LaTeX, 33 bibitems). Pre-submission hardening pass applied **5 mechanical citation fixes** (arXiv:2601.22171 author vdD ŌåÆ de Groot; arXiv:2510.13069 authors Mondino-S├żmann ŌåÆ Che/Perales/Sormani; Nieuviarts initial corrected to G.; Bo┼╝ejko-Fendler bibitem alignment; Latr├®moli├©re 2018 not 2017) ŌĆö bibliography fidelity fixes, no substantive content changes. **Concurrent-work re-check during hardening: CLEAR** ŌĆö no published Lorentzian Latr├®moli├©re-style propinquity exists as of May 2026 (verified across Latr├®moli├©re 2017/2023/2025, Hekkelman-McDonald 2024a/b, Toyota 2023, Farsi-Latr├®moli├©re 2024/2025, Leimbach-vS 2024, all strictly Riemannian; Mondino-S├żmann 2022ŌĆō2025 synthetic Lorentzian GH program is categorically different ŌĆö pre-length spaces with causal diamonds, not operator-algebraic spectral triples). **Test verification:** 316 tests pass across L3a-1 + L3b foundation + L3b-2 spot-checks (118 fast + 3 slow from v2.46.0 + new spot-checks verifying joint Plancherel factorisation and $\Nt = 1$ Riemannian-limit recovery), zero regression on any upstream baseline. **Three structural simplifications crystallised as substantive new content** (unexpected ahead of the sprint, recorded honestly): (i) PURE_TENSOR structure of the propinquity tunneling pair (L4 factorises with no cross-factor work); (ii) vanishing time-chirality cross-term $\{\gamma^{0}, \DGV\} = 0$ (L3 joint Lichnerowicz = spatial Lichnerowicz); (iii) $\Nt$-independent joint cb-norm (L2 reflects trivial central-multiplier structure of $\Uone$). The three together mean temporal compactification does not generate new analytical obstructions beyond what the foundation already handled. **Honest scope (preserved consistently):** (i) KŌü║-weak-form only ŌĆö strong-form Lorentzian propinquity (Latr├®moli├©re-style metric on Krein-signature spectral triples in their own right, without KŌü║ restriction) **remains an open NCG-math problem named as Q1** (Paper 45 ┬¦1.4 G1), requiring an indefinite-inner-product analog of the operator-norm Lipschitz seminorm; (ii) compact temporal radius $T$ canonical (BW modular period $T = 2\pi$); de-compactification $T \to \infty$ is a separate program (Sprint L3c, named gap G2); (iii) cross-manifold $\Tcal_{\sthree} \otimes \Tcal_{\mathrm{Hardy}(S^5)}$ blocked at NCG-framework level by Paper 24 ┬¦V four-layer Coulomb/HO asymmetry (named gap G3); (iv) inner-factor calibration data (Higgs / Yukawa selection) orthogonal to the present convergence theorem (named gap G4). **WH1 PROVEN status maintained** ŌĆö the Lorentzian convergence result is structurally additive on top of the proven Riemannian foundation (Paper 38), not a re-test of it. Built from sprint memos: `debug/l3b_2_sub_sprint_A_lichnerowicz_memo.md` (joint L3), `debug/l3b_2_sub_sprint_B_cb_norm_memo.md` (joint L2), `debug/l3b_2_sub_sprint_C_berezin_memo.md` (joint L4), `debug/l3b_2_sub_sprint_D_propinquity_memo.md` (joint L5), `debug/l3b_2_preflight_concurrent_work_memo.md` (related-work hardening), `debug/l3b_first_move_memo.md` (foundation, v2.46.0), `debug/l3a_1_lorentzian_operator_system_memo.md` (L1' / Paper 44). No production `geovac/` modifications (L3b foundation modules from v2.46.0 are sufficient substrate). No `tests/` modifications beyond spot-check additions. Next-direction options surfaced: (A) Sprint L3b-3 numerical-panel sweep via existing KŌü║ state-space SDP machinery (~1ŌĆō2 weeks); (B) Sprint L3c de-compactification scoping (~3ŌĆō6 weeks); (C) Strong-form Lorentzian propinquity Q1 attack (multi-month NCG-math problem); (D) return to physics-side precision catalogue or state-side dictionary work.

- **Sprint L3b-2aŌĆōd ŌĆö Strong-form Lorentzian propinquity convergence theorem (2026-05-22):** **CLOSED ŌĆö Paper 45 ┬¦1.4 Q1/G1 named open problem proved across four sub-sprints in a single multi-session day.** The strong-form Lorentzian propinquity bound ŌĆö a Latr├®moli├©re-style metric on the FULL Krein space WITHOUT KŌü║ restriction (the gap Paper 45 carried forward as the principal open NCG-math problem of the Lorentzian arc) ŌĆö is now assembled under the operator-norm Lipschitz seminorm $L_{\mathrm{op}}(a) = \|[\DL, a]\|_{\mathrm{op}}$ on the natural chirality-doubled scalar-multiplier substrate of Paper 44. **Main theorem:** $\Lambda^{\mathrm{strong}}(\Tcal^L_{\nmax, \Nt, T}, \Tcal^L_{\Manifold}) \le C_3^{\mathrm{op}}(\nmax) \cdot \gammajoint_{\nmax, \Nt, T} \to 0$ with closed-form $C_3^{\mathrm{op}}(\nmax) = \sqrt{1 - 1/\nmax} = \sqrt{(\nmax - 1)/\nmax} \to 1^-$ and rate $\gammajoint = O(\log \nmax/\nmax + T/\Nt)$ surviving verbatim from Paper 45. **Headline numerical result:** $\Lambda^{\mathrm{strong}}(2,3) = 2.0746$, $\Lambda^{\mathrm{strong}}(3,5) = 1.6101$, $\Lambda^{\mathrm{strong}}(4,7) = 1.3223$ ŌĆö **bit-exact match with Paper 45's KŌü║-weak-form values** (residual $\sim 2.4 \times 10^{-5}$ is the 4-significant-digit rounding in Paper 45 ┬¦6 Table 1; underlying $\gamma$ values match to mpmath precision). The "free-upgrade" reading is supported: the strong-form holds on the full Krein space (capturing chirality-flipping commutator content the KŌü║-weak-form discards) with the same numerical bound. **Riemannian-limit recovery at $\Nt = 1$ bit-exact** ($0.0$ residual in float64) at $\nmax \in \{2, 3, 4\}$. **Sub-sprint trajectory:** **(L3b-2a ŌĆö Candidate validation, NO-GO with substantive structural finding.)** The recommended scoping-memo candidate $L_{\mathrm{block}}(a) = \max(\|[\DL, a]|_{\Kplus}\|_{\mathrm{op}}, \|[\DL, a]|_{\Kminus}\|_{\mathrm{op}})$ is identically zero on the natural substrate (all 42 generators at $(2,3)$ and 275 generators at $(3,5)$ give $L_{\mathrm{block}}(a) = 0$ bit-exact). Diagnostic-before-engineering rule converted a 4ŌĆō6-week planned sprint into a one-day clean negative. **Substantive new content:** $\DL = D_L^{\mathrm{diag}} + D_L^{\mathrm{off}}$ where $D_L^{\mathrm{diag}} = i\gamma^0 \otimes \partial_t$ commutes with every natural-substrate generator ($[\gamma^0, M^{\mathrm{spat}}] = 0$ by Paper 44 Prop 5.1 AND $[\partial_t, M^{\mathrm{temp}}] = 0$ both momentum-diagonal ŌĆö both factors commute, not just the cross-term as Paper 45 ┬¦4.2 Lemma 4.3 used), and $D_L^{\mathrm{off}} = iD_{\mathrm{GV}} \otimes I_{\Nt}$ produces a purely chirality-flipping commutator. **The temporal direction is Lipschitz-invisible on the natural substrate** ŌĆö sharpens Paper 45 ┬¦4.2 Lemma 4.3 from "vanishing time-chirality cross-term" to "vanishing temporal commutator identically". Fallback: Candidate 1 = $L_{\mathrm{op}}$ recommended. - **Sprint L3b-2f-╬▒ ŌĆö Enlarged-substrate scoping for strong-form Lorentzian propinquity (2026-05-22):** **POSITIVE-GO** with substantive structural findings. Tests whether enlarging the operator system to chirality-flipping generators $M$ with $\{J, M\} = 0$ produces genuinely-new strong-form content beyond Paper 46's natural-substrate "free-upgrade" result. **Three independent structural identifications support the verdict:** (1) **L3b-2a structural identity BREAKS** on enlarged substrate at temporal-polynomial degree $p \ge 1$: $[D_L^{\mathrm{diag}}, a^{\mathrm{flip}}]$ becomes proportional to $2W \cdot \omega_k^p$ (non-zero), unlocking the temporal direction in the Lipschitz seminorm. (2) **Strict-strong-form separation established:** Paper 45 KŌü║-weak-form $L^+_{\mathrm{P45}}(a^{\mathrm{flip}}) = 0$ identically on chirality-flipping generators (because $P_+ M^{\mathrm{flip}} P_+ = 0$, closed-form), while $L_{\mathrm{op}}(a^{\mathrm{flip}}) > 0$. This is the genuinely-new content beyond Paper 46's natural-substrate reading. (3) **Estimated $\Lambda^{\mathrm{enlarged}}(2, 3) \approx 2.66$** vs Paper 45's $2.0746$, ratio $\sim 1.28$ ŌĆö analytical estimate consistent with Paper 46 ┬¦7.2's predicted $\sqrt{2}$ŌĆō$2$ constant range. **Construction correction (subtle but load-bearing):** the minimal anti-commuting enlargement in Paper 44's chiral-basis convention is the **chirality-asymmetric doubling $M^{\mathrm{flip}} = \mathrm{diag}(W, -W)$**, NOT the off-block-diagonal form $[[0, W], [W^*, 0]]$ that Paper 46 ┬¦7.2 abstractly described ŌĆö the distinction matters because in Paper 44's chiral basis ($\gamma^0 = [[0, I], [I, 0]]$) the off-block-diagonal form COMMUTES with $\gamma^0$ when $W$ is Hermitian (so does not anti-commute with $J$), while the asymmetric-doubling form ANTI-COMMUTES correctly. Propagation number on enlarged substrate: prop_achievable = 2 (analytical), prop_full = $\infty$ (analytical), computational verification deferred. **Environmental note:** numerical per-generator verification deferred due to persistent `geovac` module-import hangs on the local Windows machine after the first successful (2, 3) baseline run (cause unclear ŌĆö diagnostics ruled out the obvious candidates). Closed-form structural-identity diagnostic ($P_+ M^{\mathrm{flip}} P_+ = 0$, $\{J, M^{\mathrm{flip}}\} = 0$) does NOT depend on numerical run; the analytical $\Lambda^{\mathrm{enlarged}}$ estimate would benefit from stable-machine confirmation as the first step of L3b-2f-╬▓. - **Sprint L3b-2f-╬▓.1ŌĆōL5 ŌĆö Enlarged-substrate strong-form Lorentzian propinquity (2026-05-22):** **CLOSED across four sub-sprints in a single day** following the L3b-2aŌĆōd pattern. **Headline finding (the deepest structural content of the entire L3b-2f arc): the gradient-norm absorption mechanism.** The strict-strong-form separation between the enlarged substrate (chirality-asymmetric doubling $M^{\mathrm{flip}} = \mathrm{diag}(W, -W)$ in Paper 44's chiral basis, anti-commuting with $J = \gamma^0$) and Paper 45's KŌü║-weak-form substrate manifests at the Lipschitz-SEMINORM level ŌĆö $L_{\mathrm{op}}(a^{\mathrm{flip}}) > 0$ on enlarged generators while $L^+_{\mathrm{P45}}(a^{\mathrm{flip}}) = 0$ identically (since $P_+ M^{\mathrm{flip}} P_+ = 0$ closed-form) ŌĆö but this separation is paid **entirely in the GRADIENT-NORM extension** $G^{\mathrm{enlarged}}(f) := G^{\mathrm{natural}}(f) + 2\|D_t\|_{\mathrm{op}} \cdot \|f^{\mathrm{flip}}\|_{\mathrm{op}}$, leaving the Latr├®moli├©re propinquity bound bit-exactly preserved: $\Lambda^{\mathrm{enlarged}}(n_{\max}, N_t) = \Lambda^{\mathrm{P46}}(n_{\max}, N_t)$ at every panel cell. This is the cleanest possible "free upgrade" reading of the enlarged-substrate strong-form question ŌĆö deeper than Paper 46's natural-substrate free-upgrade, which still had the strict-strong-form gap open. **Sub-sprint trajectory:** **(╬▓.1 ŌĆö numerical confirmation.)** Empirical $\Lambda^{\mathrm{enlarged}}(2, 3) \approx 6.224$ (heuristic max-of-$L_{\mathrm{op}}$ estimate, NOT actual propinquity bound); strict-strong-form separation confirmed; **three substantive corrections to L3b-2f-╬▒'s analytical predictions:** (i) prop_achievable = 1 on enlarged substrate (not 2; enlarged is denser generating set, closing the achievable envelope in one step via cross-block coupling that chirality-symmetric natural substrate lacks); (ii) factor-3 = 2 + 1 closed-form decomposition (2 from $\gamma^0$-anticommutator giving $\|[\gamma^0, \mathrm{diag}(W, -W)]\|_{\mathrm{op}} = 2\|W\|_{\mathrm{op}}$, +1 from existing off-block-diagonal $D_{\mathrm{GV}}$ commutator shared with natural); (iii) L3b-2a structural identity $[D_L^{\mathrm{diag}}, a] = 0$ breaks at ALL $p$ on enlarged (not just $p \ge 1$ as ╬▒ erroneously claimed) ŌĆö root cause: ╬▒ ┬¦4.2 conflated calculus "$\partial_t \cdot 1 = 0$" with matrix algebra "$D_t \cdot I = D_t \ne 0$". - **Sprint Paper 39 k-fold extension ŌĆö CLOSED (2026-05-23):** Higher tensor factors named open question (Paper 39 ┬¦6 (iii)) promoted from "$O(\sqrt k)$ growing constant" to formal theorem at **$k$-INDEPENDENT constant**. **Substantive improvement on the CLAUDE.md estimate.** k-fold tensor-product propinquity convergence on $\mathcal{T}_{S^3}^{\lambda_1} \otimes \cdots \otimes \mathcal{T}_{S^3}^{\lambda_k}$: $\Lambda^{(k)} \le C_3^{(k)} \cdot \gamma^{(k)}$ with **$C_3^{(k)} \le \sqrt{(N_*-1)/(N_*+1)}$ where $N_* = \max_j n_j$ ŌĆö IDENTICAL to Paper 38 L3 single-factor constant, $k$-independent**, and $\gamma^{(k)} = \max_j \gamma^{\SU(2)}_{n_j}$ (worst-factor SU(2) rate, also $k$-independent). **Mechanism (substantive new content):** k-fold Pythagorean Leibniz identity $\|\sum_j X_j\|^2 = \sum_j \|X_j\|^2$ (sum-of-squares) on the Connes-Marcolli graded module, where the $k$ summands of $D^{(k)} = \sum_j \gamma_{<j} \otimes \DCH^{(j)} \otimes I_{>j}$ pairwise anti-commute. This eliminates the $\sqrt k$ Cauchy-Schwarz factor that a triangle-inequality bound would produce. Per-irrep ratio $\sum_j (N_j-1)^2 / \sum_j (N_j-1)(N_j+1) \le \max_j (N_j-1)/(N_j+1)$ via the rearrangement $\sum a_j^2 = \sum (a_j/b_j) a_j b_j \le \max_j(a_j/b_j) \sum a_j b_j$. Taking square roots gives the closed form. **Net structural finding:** k-fold tensor-product extension introduces ZERO degradation in the Lipschitz comparison constant compared to single-factor ŌĆö clean drop-in tool for arbitrary multi-focal-composition arguments at any $k$. **Asymptotic $\to 1^-$ as $\min_j n_j \to \infty$** identical to Paper 38 L3 universal $4/\pi$ rate constant. **Five-lemma transport (L1'-T-k through L5-T-k) is mechanical** from Paper 39's two-factor case. **Paper 39 ┬¦6 (iii) edit applied** (status updated from "$O(\sqrt k)$ growing" to "CLOSED with k-INDEPENDENT stronger constant"). **Paper 39 compile bug-fix bonus:** during this sprint, six pre-existing double-subscript errors on `\opnorm{T_X}_{\mathrm{cb}}` patterns (introduced at unknown earlier point, made Paper 39 uncompilable) were repaired via new `\cbnorm` macro + `microtype` disable (same fix as Papers 38/40/42/45/46/47 MiKTeX environmental issue). Paper 39 now compiles three-pass clean at 15 pages. **Honest scope:** proof rests on Connes-Marcolli graded Dirac convention (Paper 39 ┬¦3.2 ŌĆö NOT GeoVac's truthful chirality-diagonal $\DCH$); operator-algebraic / qualitative-rate level matching Paper 39's main theorem maturity; off-diagonal cutoff sharpness not addressed (mechanical sup over Avery basis gives the worst-case constant); $k=3$ numerical panel not run (mechanical extension of `geovac/gh_convergence_tensor.py` is sprint-scale follow-on if PI wants empirical confirmation). Files: `debug/sprint_paper39_k_fold_extension_memo.md` (~3500 words, 8 sections).

- **Sprint Pythagorean Orthogonality ŌĆö formal proof of $\langle H_{\mathrm{local}}, D_W^L\rangle_{HS} = 0$ (2026-05-23):** **CLOSED at the operator-algebraic level via $\mathbb{Z}_2$ wedge-chirality parity argument.** Promotes the L2-F.1 (2026-05-17) "structural sketch" of the subspace-decomposition mechanism to a formal Theorem (Paper 43 ┬¦10.2 Theorem `thm:pythagorean_formal`), closing the Paper 43 ┬¦11 O4 named follow-on. **Theorem:** under the BW construction at finite $(n_{\max}, N_t)$, $\langle H_{\mathrm{local}}, D_W^L\rangle_{HS} = \mathrm{Tr}_{\mathcal{K}_W}(H_{\mathrm{local}}^\dagger D_W^L) = 0$ as an exact operator-algebraic identity. **Three structural inputs from Papers 42/43/44:** (I1) wedge chirality grading $\Pi_W$ (BBB $\gamma^5$ restricted to wedge) is a unitary self-adjoint involution; (I2) $[\Pi_W, H_{\mathrm{local}}] = 0$ (even parity ŌĆö $K_\alpha^W = J_{\mathrm{polar}}^W$ acts by $m_j$-dependent eigenvalues independent of chirality); (I3) $\{\Pi_W, D_W^L\} = 0$ (odd parity ŌĆö both factors of $D_L = i(\gamma^0 \otimes \partial_t + D_{\mathrm{GV}} \otimes I)$ are $\Pi_W$-odd: $\gamma^0$ anticommutes with $\gamma^5$ in chiral basis; truthful chirality-diagonal $D_{\mathrm{GV}}$ becomes off-diagonal in unfolded-wedge basis via L2-F.1 basis change). **Lemma (parity / HS-orthogonality):** if $\Pi$ is a unitary involution, $[\Pi, A] = 0$, $\{\Pi, B\} = 0$, then $\mathrm{Tr}(A^\dagger B) = 0$ via cyclicity-of-trace and unitary-conjugation invariance ($\mathrm{Tr}(X) = \mathrm{Tr}(\Pi X \Pi^{-1})$). **Net structural finding:** the bit-exact $\langle H_{\mathrm{local}}, D_W^L\rangle_{HS} = 0$ at 18 panel cells (L2-F.1) is no longer empirical ŌĆö it is the exact algebraic identity forced by the BW-construction $\mathbb{Z}_2$ parity grading. Pythagorean closed form $r^2 = \|H_{\mathrm{local}}\|_F^2 + \|D_W^L\|_F^2$ follows as immediate corollary. **Universality across six modular witnesses** (BW + HH├Ś2 + Sew + Unruh├Ś2) is automatic: witnesses parameterize $\kappa_g$ which rescales $H_{\mathrm{local}}$ within its $\Pi_W$-even subspace, cannot rotate it into the $\Pi_W$-odd subspace where $D_W^L$ sits. **Honest scope (preserved):** (i) proof rests on the three structural inputs from Papers 42/43/44 ŌĆö granular derivation from CH matrix elements is a sub-sprint follow-on; (ii) finite cutoff only, continuum limit requires Paper 47's two-rate hybrid; (iii) wedge only, cross-manifold $T_{S^3} \otimes T_{\mathrm{Hardy}(S^5)}$ remains G3 blocker. **Paper 43 edits applied (same session):** ┬¦10.2 promoted from "structural sketch" with named follow-on to formal Theorem block (Lemma `lem:parity_HS` + Theorem `thm:pythagorean_formal` + proof + three inputs I1/I2/I3 + honest scope); ┬¦11 O4 status updated from "formal proof named follow-on" to "now formally closed by Theorem `thm:pythagorean_formal`"; Paper 43 grew 24ŌåÆ25 pages, three-pass clean compile, zero substantive warnings. **WH1 PROVEN status maintained** ŌĆö Pythagorean orthogonality formal proof is structurally additive within the Lorentzian arc (Papers 43 / 45 / 46 / 47), not a re-test of any foundation. - **Sprint L3c ŌĆö De-compactification limit $T \to \infty$, G2 closure at norm-resolvent level + Paper 47 (2026-05-23):** **CLOSED at the norm-resolvent / spectral level via a three-sub-sprint arc in a single session.** Closes Paper 45 ┬¦1.4 G2 (de-compactification limit) at the appropriate convergence-notion level for GeoVac's current scope; metric-level propinquity closure on the non-compact carrier remains open as G2-metric / G1-genuine (multi-month frontier). **(Scoping memo, sprint L3c)** four-sub-sprint architecture identified: L3c-╬▒ (parametric stability on natural substrate, 3ŌĆō5 wk LOW risk), L3c-╬▓ (enlarged substrate, 6ŌĆō10 wk MEDIUM, deferred per ╬▓-L3's $O(T)$ obstruction), L3c-╬│ (inductive-limit / non-compact-target convergence, 6ŌĆō10 wk MED-HIGH), L3c-╬┤ (full non-compact Latr├®moli├©re propinquity, multi-month frontier). **(L3c-╬▒, CLOSED)** Parametric propinquity stability on natural substrate: for any admissible scaling $T(N_t) \to \infty$ with $T(N_t)/N_t \to 0$, $\Lprop(\mathcal{T}^L_{n_{\max}, N_t, T(N_t)}, \mathcal{T}^L_{S^3 \times S^1_{T(N_t)}}) \le C_3^{\mathrm{joint}}(n_{\max}) \cdot \gamma^{\mathrm{joint}} \to 0$. **Load-bearing observation:** every $T$-dependent quantity in Paper 45's propinquity bound is concentrated in L4's $\gamma^{U(1)} = O(T/N_t)$ Fej├®r-on-circle rate; all other constants ($C_3^{\mathrm{joint}}$, cb-norm, propagation number, reach/height structure) are structurally $T$-independent on the natural substrate via the L3 structural identity $[\DL, a_s \otimes a_t] = i[\DGV, a_s] \otimes a_t$ (Paper 45 eq:L3_struct_id). Per-lemma audit: L1' L2 L3 L5 transport TRIVIAL; L4 transports under admissible scaling. Analytical corollary of Paper 45/46 main theorem, no new analytical content beyond parametric reformulation. **(L3c-╬│, CLOSED ŌĆö substantive new content)** Norm-resolvent convergence $\mathcal{T}^L_{S^3 \times S^1_T} \to \mathcal{T}^L_{S^3 \times \R_t}$ as $T \to \infty$ with explicit exponential tail $O(e^{-|\Im z| T/2})$ on compact-temporal-support subspaces. **Strategic reframing (substantive sprint content):** the original L3c-╬│ framing as "AF inductive-limit propinquity" (Latr├®moli├©re 2018 ┬¦5) was structurally wrong because $\R$ is connected but AF C*-algebras have totally-disconnected spectrum ŌĆö therefore $C_0(\R)$ cannot be an AF inductive limit; the AF inductive limit of $\{C(S^1_{T_n})\}$ along $T_n = 2^n T_0$ refinement chains is a Bunce-Deddens-style algebra, not $C_0(\R)$. The right framework is norm-resolvent convergence (Connes 1994 ┬¦VI), which captures spectral data and operator-algebraic structure but NOT Lipschitz/metric structure ŌĆö appropriate for G2's physical content ("the Lorentzian Dirac on the compactified spacetime converges to the Lorentzian Dirac on the genuine spacetime") at the level GeoVac currently supports. Four-step proof: (1) spatial factorization reduces to temporal-only convergence; (2) Reed-Simon Vol. IV ┬¦XIII.16 / Bloch-decomposition compact-to-noncompact-domain machinery with explicit Poisson-summation form of periodic resolvent kernel; (3) tensor-product extension to full Krein space; (4) Krein-self-adjointness preserved via $\widetilde J_T : L^2(S^1_T) \hookrightarrow L^2(\R)$ Krein-isometric embedding ($\widetilde J_T^* \JL_\R \widetilde J_T = \JL_T$ bit-exact, KŌü║-cone preserved). **(Composite L3c-╬▒ + L3c-╬│, the headline two-rate hybrid result)** $\mathcal{T}^L_{n_{\max}, N_t, T(N_t)} \xrightarrow{\Lprop\text{-rate}} \mathcal{T}^L_{S^3 \times S^1_{T(N_t)}} \xrightarrow{\mathrm{nr}\text{-rate}} \mathcal{T}^L_{S^3 \times \R_t}$ at rates $O(\log n_{\max}/n_{\max} + T(N_t)/N_t)$ inner and $O(e^{-|\Im z| T(N_t)/2})$ outer. The two rates do NOT compose into a single uniform Latr├®moli├©re bound (one is propinquity, the other is norm-resolvent ŌĆö different convergence notions) but they do give a joint statement of finite-cutoff Lorentzian Dirac convergence to the genuine non-compact Lorentzian Dirac. **(Three-carrier identification, substantive Paper 47 ┬¦6 content)** Three nominally distinct Lorentzian Krein carriers ŌĆö periodic compact $S^3 \times S^1_T$ (Paper 45 architecture), bounded Dirichlet $S^3 \times [-T/2, T/2]$ (Paper 43 / L2-B/E architecture), non-compact $S^3 \times \R_t$ (Paper 47 limit) ŌĆö all converge in norm-resolvent sense to the same physical Lorentzian Dirac as $T \to \infty$. ## 3. Approaches That Failed

Critical institutional memory. Do not re-derive these dead ends. Full details in CHANGELOG.md. Sub-agents must check CHANGELOG.md before attempting any approach in these categories.

| Category | Count | Key Lesson |
|:---------|:-----:|:-----------|
| LCAO / single-S┬│ molecular encoding | 3 | Graph Laplacian kinetic energy is R-independent; need natural geometry where separation occurs |
| PK modifications (projector, spectral, self-consistent, R-dependent, l-dependent on 2D) | 6 | PK provides coordinate-space exclusion that angular projectors categorically cannot replicate; PK is the irreducible cost of composed-geometry factorization |
| Cusp treatments (alpha-only, graph absorption, ╬ĖŌéüŌéé-adapted basis) | 3 | Cusp is 2D in (╬▒, ╬ĖŌéüŌéé); 1/rŌéüŌéé is an embedding exchange constant; Schwartz extrapolation is the correct approach |
| Inter-group antisymmetry (node exclusion, fiber bundle, spectral) | 3 | Antisymmetry requires shared coordinate system; composed geometry factorizes into incompatible coordinates |
| Full N-electron radial solvers (adiabatic, coupled-channel, 2D variational) | 3 | Adiabatic overcounts D_e; coupled-channel numerically unstable; 2D gives unbound D_e; angular basis is the bottleneck |
| Polyatomic coupling (Z_eff partition, classical repulsion, lone pair at Z_eff>4) | 3 | Orbital-level exchange coupling needed; lone pair Slater integrals unphysical at high Z_eff |

Single-point energy also diverges, violating variational bound. l_max=2 is optimal. |

## 3.5. Guardrail Papers

Certain papers contain proven theorems or exhaustive diagnostic arcs that constrain what approaches are viable. Sub-agents MUST load the relevant guardrail paper before beginning any investigation in the constrained domain. If a proposed investigation falls within a guardrail's scope, the sub-agent must:

1. Load the guardrail paper into context
2. Identify the specific theorem or negative result that applies
3. WARN THE USER: "Paper [X] documents a proven negative result for this class of approach: [theorem statement]. The proposed investigation [specific proposal] appears to fall within scope. Do you want to proceed anyway, or modify the approach?"
4. If the user proceeds: document in the investigation prompt that the guardrail was acknowledged and state why the new attempt differs from the documented negative result

This protocol exists because Track DF (6 sprints, April 2026) re-derived at significant cost two negative results that were already proven in Papers 8-9 and FCI-M. The re-derivation produced genuine new findings (6j sparsity theorem, compact encoding, three-layer structure), but Sprints 4 and 4B could have been avoided entirely if the guardrail papers had been loaded at the investigation design stage.

### Current Guardrail Papers

| Paper | Domain | Theorem/Result | Scope |
|:------|:-------|:---------------|:------|
| Paper 8-9 | Single-center molecular encoding | Sturmian Structural Theorem: H_ij ŌłØ S_ij in shared-pŌéĆ basis ŌåÆ eigenvalues R-independent | ANY investigation proposing to encode a heteronuclear molecule in a single-center (single-Z, single-k, single-pŌéĆ) basis, including nested hyperspherical, bond sphere, Sturmian CI, or unified orbital approaches |
| FCI-M | Graph-concatenation molecular encoding | Graph Laplacian kinetic energy is R-independent in LCAO basis ŌåÆ monotonically attractive PES, no equilibrium | ANY investigation proposing to concatenate atom-centered graphs into a molecular graph without natural geometry coordinates |
| Track DF record | Nested hyperspherical molecular encoding | Three molecular variants tested (single-center, charge-center, heterogeneous L├Čwdin) ŌĆö all NEGATIVE | ANY investigation proposing to place all molecular electrons in a single S^(3N-1) Hilbert space. Extends Paper 8-9's theorem to the hyperspherical setting with additional finding: L├Čwdin orthogonalization of mixed-exponent bases destroys Gaunt sparsity |

### Guardrail Triggers

When a user or investigation prompt proposes work in any of the following categories, the sub-agent MUST load the indicated guardrail paper BEFORE writing any implementation plan:

- **"single center" + "molecule"** ŌåÆ Load Papers 8-9
- **"unified basis" + "molecule"** ŌåÆ Load Papers 8-9
- **"shared exponent" OR "single k" OR "single pŌéĆ" + "molecule"** ŌåÆ Load Papers 8-9
- **"nested" + "molecule"** ŌåÆ Load Papers 8-9 + Track DF record
- **"graph" + "concatenat"** ŌåÆ Load FCI-M
- **"LCAO" + "graph"** ŌåÆ Load FCI-M
- **"Sturmian" + "molecule"** ŌåÆ Load Papers 8-9

After loading, the sub-agent must check whether the proposed approach falls within the guardrail's scope and warn the user if it does. The warning should be constructive, not blocking ŌĆö it documents what DOESN'T work, which helps refine toward what MIGHT work.

---

## 4. The Dimensionless Vacuum Principle

The graph Laplacian is dimensionless and scale-invariant, topologically equivalent to the unit three-sphere S3. Physical energies emerge only through the energy-shell constraint p0^2 = -2E, which acts as a stereographic focal length. The 1/r Coulomb potential is not an input force law -- it is the coordinate distortion from stereographic projection (chordal distance identity). The universal kinetic scale kappa = -1/16 maps graph eigenvalues to the Rydberg spectrum. Eigenvalues of the Laplace-Beltrami operator on unit S3 are pure integers: lambda_n = -(n^2 - 1).

For molecules, the natural geometry shifts from S3 (atoms) to prolate spheroidal coordinates (Paper 11), hyperspherical coordinates (Paper 13), molecule-frame hyperspherical (Paper 15), or composed fiber bundles (Paper 17). The choice of geometry is determined by where separation of variables occurs. At Level 1, the separated coordinates are all angular (on S3), making the problem fully discrete. At Levels 2+, separation produces continuous radial-like coordinates alongside discrete angular channels ŌĆö a consequence of SO(4) symmetry breaking by multi-center or multi-electron potentials (Papers 8-9, negative theorem).

**Prime directive (level-aware):** The framework preserves two distinct kinds of structure, and the rules differ by level:

*Angular/symmetry structure (discrete at all levels):* The quantum number labeling (n, l, m), the per-shell degeneracy 2l+1, the selection rules from Gaunt integrals, and the channel structure are combinatorial invariants derived from the packing construction (Paper 0). These must never be modified, approximated, or bypassed at any level. They are the framework's core identity.

*Radial/parametric structure (level-dependent):* At Level 1, Fock's SO(4) symmetry converts the radial coordinate into an angular coordinate on S3, making the entire problem discrete. The graph Laplacian is the exact object and must not be modified to artificially recover continuous differential terms (like 1/r or nabla^2). At Levels 2-4, the SO(4) symmetry is broken by multi-center or multi-electron physics, and the radial-like coordinates (internuclear distance R, hyperradius R_e, prolate spheroidal xi) currently require continuous numerical methods. However, this is not necessarily a fundamental feature of the physics ŌĆö it may reflect algebraic structures that haven't been found yet. The project has already demonstrated this replacement in several cases: Paper 12's Neumann expansion replaced numerical quadrature of V_ee with algebraic recurrence relations; Gaunt integrals replace angular integration at all levels; the split-region Legendre expansion (Paper 15) terminates exactly via the 3j triangle inequality. In each case, what appeared to require continuous integration was replaced by algebraic evaluation once the right structure was identified.

The places where continuous numerical methods currently survive are: Z_eff screening quadrature in composed geometries, spline caching for the rho-collapse, finite-difference radial grids in hyperspherical solvers, and the adiabatic potential curves U(R). These are computational tools for evaluating coupling matrix elements between discrete channel structures. Standard numerical methods (grid refinement, basis convergence, quadrature improvement) are appropriate for improving accuracy in these areas. Finding algebraic replacements for these numerical steps ŌĆö as Paper 12 did for V_ee ŌĆö is an ongoing goal of the project.

The framework's long-term aspiration is: for every natural geometry, there exists an algebraic structure that computes all coupling matrix elements without spatial integration. This has been achieved for Level 1 (S3 graph eigenvalues), for angular couplings at all levels (Gaunt integrals), and for electron-electron repulsion in prolate spheroidal coordinates (Neumann expansion). It has not yet been achieved for the hyperradial coupling in Levels 3-4 or for Z_eff screening in Level 5. What must be preserved at every level is the discrete channel structure and selection rules, not the specific numerical method used to evaluate radial amplitudes within those channels.

**Algebraic-first, observation-aware (refinement after Papers 18 / 34, May 2026):** The aspiration above is the right discipline for Layer 1 (the bare graph) and for the discrete channel structure at every level. After Paper 34's two-layer framing, the project distinguishes algebraic content (Layer 1: ŽĆ-free, integer / rational / algebraic-extension matrix elements) from observation-side content (Layer 2: where projections to physical observables introduce specific transcendentals ŌĆö ŽĆ via the Hopf measure, ŽĆ^{2k} via the spectral action, ╬Č(2k) via even-zeta Dirichlet series, ╬Č(3) via half-integer Hurwitz, Catalan G via vertex parity, 2ŽĆ via temporal compactification when an observer integrates over a finite time window). Irreducible transcendentals that survive algebraic decomposition are not failures of the algebraic-first discipline ŌĆö they are the *content* of a specific Paper 34 projection and should be pinned to that projection rather than chased indefinitely. The diagnostic question for any quadrature wall is therefore two-headed: (i) is the wall a missing algebraic structure (decompose, per Paper 12 / cross-block V_ne / hypergeometric Slater), or (ii) is it the irreducible signature of an observation-side projection (catalogue against Paper 34 and stop)? Both answers are valid outcomes; conflating them was the error the May-2026 curve-fit audit flagged.

*Practical test:* If a proposed modification changes which quantum numbers label the states or which transitions are allowed, it violates the prime directive. If it changes how accurately the radial amplitude is computed within a given channel, it is a legitimate numerical improvement. If it adds a transcendental, the transcendental must be tagged to a Paper 34 projection ŌĆö anonymous transcendentals are not allowed in production code or papers.

**Topological integrity tests:** The 18 symbolic proofs in `tests/test_fock_projection.py` and `tests/test_fock_laplacian.py` validate S3 conformal geometry. These must never be broken or bypassed. Run before any release.

---

## 5. Natural Geometry Hierarchy

The core organizational principle of the project. Each electron configuration has a natural coordinate system where the physics separates.

| Level | System | Natural Geometry | Best Result | Paper |
|:-----:|:-------|:-----------------|:------------|:-----:|
| 1 | H (1-center, 1e) | S3 (Fock) | < 0.1% | 7 |
| 2 | H2+ (2-center, 1e) | Prolate spheroid | 0.0002% (spectral) | 11 |
| 3 | He (1-center, 2e) | Hyperspherical | 0.019% (2D var + self-consistent cusp); 0.20% (graph-native CI n_max=9, 0 params, exact algebraic integrals) | 13 |

*Level 3 note:* The previous 0.05% result used the FD adiabatic solver (lucky error cancellation, non-variational). The adiabatic coupled-channel solver converges to a structural floor of 0.19-0.20% (v2.0.8). The 2D variational solver (Track DI, v2.6.0) breaks this floor: raw 0.022% at l_max=7 (tensor-product Laguerre ├Ś Gegenbauer basis, 8000 dim), cusp-corrected 0.004% at l_max=4. The 2D solver treats R and ╬▒ simultaneously, capturing non-adiabatic R-╬▒ correlation that the adiabatic approximation misses. l_max convergence is monotonic; the per-channel angular basis (n_basis=40 Gegenbauer functions) is the convergence bottleneck, not partial-wave truncation.
| 4 | H2 (2-center, 2e) | Mol-frame hyperspherical | 96.0% D_e | 15 |
| 4N | LiH (2-center, 4e) | Full mol-frame hypersp. (SO(12)) | R_eq 63.5% (l_max=2, 2D variational; unbound D_e) | 17 |
| 5 | LiH (core+valence) | Composed (Level 3 + 4) | R_eq 5.3% | 17 |
| 5 | BeHŌéé (polyatomic) | Composed (Level 3 + 4) + exchange | R_eq 11.7% | 17 |
| 5 | HŌééO (triatomic) | Composed (Level 3 + 4) + lone pairs | R_eq 26% | 17 |
| Nested | Be (1-center, 4e) | S┬╣┬╣ (SO(12)), H-set | Q=10, 112 Pauli, 4.9% | Track DF |

*Level 4N note:* Level 4N is the exact N-electron generalization of Level 4's mol-frame hyperspherical coordinates (SO(3N) replacing SO(6), S_N antisymmetry replacing the gerade constraint). Level 5 (composed geometry) approximates Level 4N, trading exact inter-group antisymmetry for 144x angular compression via PK. The l_max=2 result (R_eq Ōēł 1.1 bohr, 63.5% error) demonstrates that equilibrium exists without PK. Track AR (v2.0.23) confirmed that D_e overcounting was an adiabatic artifact: the 2D variational solver gives E_min = -7.79 Ha (variational bound respected, above exact -8.07) with D_e = -0.19 Ha (unbound), versus the adiabatic solver's D_e = +0.49 Ha (5.3x exact). The l_max=2 SŌéä [2,2] angular basis is genuinely insufficient for LiH binding. Track AS (v2.0.23) confirmed composed encoding is categorically sparser than full N-electron encoding (334 vs 3,288 Pauli terms, 20x lower 1-norm). Composed geometry's 144x angular compression and structural sparsity are essential, not approximations of convenience.

The composed geometry (Level 5) is a fiber bundle: G_total = G_nuc semi-direct G_core(R) semi-direct G_val(R, core_state). Each electron group gets its own natural coordinate system, coupled via Z_eff screening and Phillips-Kleinman pseudopotential.

**Algebraic structure:** At every level, angular matrix elements are computed from quantum number labels and Wigner 3j symbols (via Gaunt integrals), with no spatial quadrature. The split-region Legendre expansion (Paper 15) terminates exactly via the 3j triangle inequality. At Level 2, the radial solver is fully algebraic for all m: Žā states (m=0) use ordinary Laguerre three-term recurrence with zero numerical integration (v2.0.9); ŽĆ/╬┤ states (mŌēĀ0) use associated Laguerre basis L_n^{|m|}(x) with partial-fraction decomposition and Stieltjes integral recurrence, reducing non-algebraic content to a single transcendental seed e^a┬ĘEŌéü(a) (Track J, v2.0.10). At Level 3, the angular problem is fully algebraic, and the hyperradial overlap S and kinetic K matrices are algebraic via three-term Laguerre recurrence (Track H, v2.0.10: pentadiagonal M2 for S, tridiagonal derivative expansion for K, < 1e-14 relative error, 11├Ś build speedup). The adiabatic eigenvalues ╬╝(R) are proven transcendental (O(R) ŌåÆ O(R┬▓) regime transition, v2.0.9 Track G) ŌĆö the potential V_eff(R) must stay quadrature, point-by-point diagonalization is irreducible, though spectral radial solvers achieve 95-120├Ś speedups. At Level 4, the spectral Laguerre basis achieves 16├Ś dimension reduction for the hyperradial coordinate (Track I), and the spectral Jacobi basis achieves 20├Ś dimension reduction for the angular sweep (Track K, 269├Ś speedup, 1000ŌåÆ50 matrix dimension). The combined spectral solver reduces the angular sweep from 99% to ~50% of total cost. The angular eigenvalues ╬╝(Žü) remain transcendental (computed by diagonalization at each Žü-point), but the per-point cost is now a 50├Ś50 eigensolve rather than a 1000├Ś1000 one. n_basis_radial=20 optimal (mild conditioning at n_basisŌēź25). Spatial quadrature enters for: Level 3 hyperradial potential matrix elements (V_eff transcendental), Level 4 angular eigenvalue sweeps (╬╝(Žü) transcendental, but spectral basis reduces cost 269├Ś), Z_eff screening in composed geometries, and rho-collapse spline caching.

| 4 | Archived 2026-05-03 | `Paper_4_Universality.tex` | Universal holographic central charge / muonic-hydrogen / proton-radius-puzzle resolution. Archived because (1) proton radius puzzle resolved by measurement (PDG 0.8409(4) fm), and (2) holographic claims inherit Paper 3 retraction. Salvageable kernel (mass as unit-fixing projection) absorbed into Paper 34/35. |
| 5 | Conjecture | `Paper_5_Geometric_Vacuum.tex` | Comprehensive geometric vacuum framework (early synthesis) |
| 6 | Archived 2026-05-22 | `Paper_6_Quantum_Dynamics.tex` | O(V) quantum dynamics on the graph (Rabi, spectroscopy, AIMD). Archived because cross-group dependency analysis (2026-05-22) showed 1-in/1-out citation pattern ŌĆö essentially orphan in the corpus. Content remains valid as a tool paper; load on explicit request when graph-dynamics tooling is needed. |
| 10 | Archive | `paper_10_nuclear_lattice.tex` | Rovibrational spectra from SU(2) algebraic chains (early draft) |
| 18 v1 | Superseded | `paper_18_exchange_constants_v1.tex` | Earlier version of Paper 18; superseded by current `papers/group3_foundations/paper_18_exchange_constants.tex` |
| 21 | Archived 2026-05-22 | `paper_21_geometric_vacuum_synthesis.tex` | Early synthesis: S┬│ proof chain, N-electron S^(3N-1), exchange constant taxonomy, 6j recoupling sparsity, Hopf ╬▒ conjecture. Archived because cross-group dependency analysis showed only 1 inbound citation across the entire corpus AND because the two new group syntheses (`papers/synthesis/group1_operator_algebras_synthesis.tex` and `papers/synthesis/group3_foundations_synthesis.tex`) supersede its narrative role with explicit cross-group framing. Content remains valid as a historical snapshot. |

## 7. Code Architecture

### Key Entry Points

| Task | Module | Entry Point |
|:-----|:-------|:------------|
| Atomic lattice | `geovac/lattice.py` | `GeometricLattice(Z, max_n)` |
| Atomic Hamiltonian | `geovac/hamiltonian.py` | `GraphHamiltonian(lattice)` |
| Multi-electron FCI | `geovac/lattice_index.py` | `LatticeIndex(Z, n_electrons, max_n)` |
| Direct CI (large systems) | `geovac/direct_ci.py` | `DirectCISolver(lattice_index)` |
| Molecular FCI (LCAO) | `geovac/lattice_index.py` | `MolecularLatticeIndex(atoms, R)` |
| Prolate spheroidal (H2+) | `geovac/prolate_spheroidal.py` | Prolate spheroidal lattice for diatomics |
| Hyperspherical (He) | `geovac/hyperspherical.py` | Two-electron hyperspherical solver |
| Level 4 (H2) | `geovac/level4_multichannel.py` | Molecule-frame hyperspherical |
| Core screening | `geovac/core_screening.py` | `CoreScreening(Z).solve()` |
| Ab initio PK | `geovac/ab_initio_pk.py` | `AbInitioPK(core, n_core)` |
| Composed diatomic | `geovac/composed_diatomic.py` | `ComposedDiatomicSolver.LiH_ab_initio(l_max)` |
| Rho-collapse cache | `geovac/rho_collapse_cache.py` | `AngularCache`, `FastAdiabaticPES` |
| Quantum dynamics | `geovac/dynamics.py` | O(V) time evolution |
| Hopf bundle | `geovac/hopf_bundle.py` | S3 embedding, Hopf projection, fiber analysis |
| VQE benchmark | `geovac/vqe_benchmark.py` | `build_geovac_he()`, `run_vqe()`, `collect_static_metrics()` |
| Gaussian reference | `geovac/gaussian_reference.py` | `h2_sto3g()`, `he_sto3g()`, `he_cc_pvdz()`, `he_cc_pvtz()` |

### Solver Methods

| Method | Access | Use Case |
|:-------|:-------|:---------|
| Mean-field | `LatticeIndex(method='mean_field')` | Quick atomic energies |
| Full CI (matrix) | `LatticeIndex(method='full_ci')` | Small systems (N_SD < 5000) |
| Full CI (direct) | `DirectCISolver` or `fci_method='direct'` | Large systems (N_SD >= 5000) |
| Auto | `fci_method='auto'` | Switches at N_SD = 5000 |
| Frozen core | `FrozenCoreLatticeIndex` | Active-space CI for core-valence |
| Locked shell | `LockedShellMolecule` | Extreme SD reduction for heavy atoms |

---

## 8. Coding Standards

### Sparse vs Dense: Context-Dependent

- **Hamiltonian and CI matrices (N > 100):** Always `scipy.sparse` (csr_matrix, coo_matrix). Never densify.
- **Hot-loop lookup tables (ERI, h1 in direct CI):** Use dense NumPy when array fits in memory (n_spinorb <= ~300). `scipy.sparse._validate_indices` overhead (~24us/call) is prohibitive at 100K+ lookups.

Rule of thumb: sparse for the physics matrix (N_SD x N_SD), dense for orbital-index lookup tables (n_spinorb x n_spinorb or n_spatial^4).

### Type Hints Required

All function signatures must have type hints.

```python
def compute_ground_state(self, n_states: int = 1) -> Tuple[np.ndarray, np.ndarray]:
    ...
```

### Physical Constants

Import from `geovac.constants` or define at module top. No hardcoded magic numbers.
**Exception:** `-1/16` is the universal topological constant (can be used directly).

### Vectorization Over Loops

Avoid Python loops for graph operations; use NumPy masking/vectorization.

```python
mask = (n_values >= 1) & (l_values < n_values)
states_filtered = states[mask]
```

---

## 9. Workflow Protocols

### Theory Check Rule

Before implementing new physics:
1. Check `papers/` for the derivation
2. If code contradicts paper -> flag it and ask user
3. If changing physics in code -> prompt user to update papers

### Benchmarking Rule

After any modification to `hamiltonian.py`, `lattice.py`, or `solver.py`:
1. Run topological integrity: `pytest tests/test_fock_projection.py tests/test_fock_laplacian.py -v`
2. Run validation: `pytest tests/advanced_benchmarks.py`
3. Verify 18/18 symbolic proofs pass (topological foundation)
4. Verify H2+ < 0.1% error (topological control)
5. Verify H2 Full CI < 1.0% error (accuracy control)
6. Report any speed regression > 10%

### Clean Room Rule

- Generated plots -> `debug/plots/` or `papers/figures/`
- Generated data -> `debug/data/`
- Scripts -> `debug/`, `demo/`, `tests/`, or `benchmarks/` (never root)
- Documentation -> `docs/`

### Changelog Protocol

**Changelog granularity:** Each CHANGELOG entry should correspond to a releasable unit of work ŌĆö a new feature, a completed diagnostic arc, a paper update, or a benchmark result. Do not create a new version entry for intermediate debugging steps, parameter sweeps, or exploratory runs. If a task requires multiple iterations to complete, document it as a single entry when the task concludes, noting the key findings and negative results. Intermediate data belongs in `debug/` with timestamped filenames, not in the CHANGELOG.

**Version numbering:** Patch versions (x.y.Z) for bug fixes and documentation; minor versions (x.Y.0) for new features, completed diagnostic arcs, or paper additions; major versions (X.0.0) for architectural changes. A diagnostic arc that tests 10 hypotheses and finds 9 negative results is one minor version, not 10 patches.

---

## 12. Algebraic Registry

Tracks which matrix elements at each level are computed algebraically vs numerically. Status: **algebraic** (closed-form from quantum numbers), **algebraic (implicit)** (defined by polynomial equation P=0 with known coefficient ring; pointwise diag is computational convenience, not mathematical necessity), **algebraic-pending** (algebraic route identified but production code still uses quadrature), **numerical-required** (no known algebraic replacement).

### Level 3 (Hyperspherical ŌĆö He)

| Matrix Element | Status | Notes |
|:---------------|:------:|:------|
| SO(6) Casimir eigenvalues | algebraic | Exact: ╬Į(╬Į+4)/2 from representation theory |
| Centrifugal barrier | algebraic | Diagonal in Gegenbauer spectral basis (confirmed Track B, v2.0.6) |
| Nuclear coupling | algebraic | Partial harmonic sums (Eqs. 31-32, Paper 13) |
| V_ee coupling | algebraic-pending | Split-region Legendre structure confirmed; GL quadrature still used in production |
| Centrifugal matrix elements | algebraic | Diagonal in Gegenbauer basis (v2.0.6) |
| Hyperradial overlap (S) | algebraic | Pentadiagonal M2 moment matrix from three-term Laguerre recurrence. S = M2/(8╬▒┬│). Machine-precision agreement with quadrature (< 1e-14 relative). (Track H, v2.0.10) |
| Hyperradial kinetic (K) | algebraic | Derivative kernel B_n = -n/2 L_{n-1} + 1/2 L_n + (n+1)/2 L_{n+1} (tridiagonal). K = bbßĄĆ/(4╬▒). Machine-precision agreement (< 1e-14 relative). 11├Ś build speedup. (Track H, v2.0.10) |
| Hyperradial potential (V_eff) | algebraic at l_max=0; numerical-required at l_maxŌēź1 | l_max=0: V_eff algebraic via Stieltjes moment decomposition (single transcendental seed e^a┬ĘEŌéü(a), Track P2 v2.0.13). l_maxŌēź1: ╬╝(R) is algebraic over Q(ŽĆ,ŌłÜ2) (Track P1), but V_eff integrals are non-elementary (radical obstruction: ŌłÜ╬ö(R) at l_max=1, Cardano at l_max=2). Quadrature required. |
| Hellmann-Feynman P-matrix | algebraic | Exact from R-independent dH/dR (v2.0.6) |
| Q-matrix (second derivative coupling) | algebraic | Exact Q = PP + dP/dR computed from Hellmann-Feynman quantities (v2.0.6) |
| Coupled-channel radial solve | numerical-required | Coupled ODE integration on R grid |
| Adiabatic potential curves U(R) | algebraic (implicit) | ╬╝(R) satisfies P(R,╬╝)=0, polynomial in both R and ╬╝, coefficients in Q(ŽĆ,ŌłÜ2)[R]. Degree L+1 in both variables at l_max=L. Point-by-point diagonalization is computational convenience. (Track P1, v2.0.12) |
| TC double commutator | algebraic | [[H, R sin(╬▒)], R sin(╬▒)] = -kron(S_R, I + cos┬▓╬▒). Exact closed form, terminates at 2nd order for 2 electrons. The cos┬▓╬▒ matrix is block-diagonal in l (Y_l orthogonality). |
| TC single commutator | algebraic | [H, R sin(╬▒)] = (-d/dR)ŌŖŚsin(╬▒) + (1/R)ŌŖŚ[╬ø┬▓+15/8, sin(╬▒)] + IŌŖŚ[C, sin(╬▒)]. D_R via Laguerre derivative (x weight, anti-symmetric). Angular commutator via IBP + V_extra decomposition. |
| Angular Casimir decomposition | algebraic | V_extra = diag(casimir) - IBP_free, where IBP_free[j,k] = <Žć_j'|Žć_k'>. Extracts the SŌü┤ metric cotangent-derivative terms algebraically from the known eigenvalues. Angular derivatives from d/du C_n^╬╗(u) = 2╬╗ C_{n-1}^{╬╗+1}(u). |
| sin/sin┬▓/cos┬▓ angular matrices | algebraic | Block-diagonal in l by Y_l(╬ĖŌéüŌéé) orthogonality. Cross-channel elements are zero because sin(╬▒) preserves ╬ĖŌéüŌéé quantum number l. (v2.8.2) |

### Level 2 (Prolate Spheroidal ŌĆö HŌééŌü║)

| Matrix Element | Status | Notes |
|:---------------|:------:|:------|
| Angular ╬Ę-eigenfunctions | algebraic | Legendre spectral basis (n_basis=50), same as Mitnik et al. angular component |
| Azimuthal m | algebraic | Exact separation of variables, integer quantum number |
| Radial ╬Š-solver (m=0) | algebraic | Ordinary Laguerre basis (n_basis=20, ╬▒-adapted). 250├Ś dimension reduction vs FD. Three-term recurrence for ALL matrix elements ŌĆö zero quadrature. Machine-precision agreement with quadrature (< 1e-14). (v2.0.9) |
| Radial ╬Š-solver (mŌēĀ0) | algebraic | Associated Laguerre basis L_n^{|m|}(x) with weight x^|m|┬Ęe^{-x}. Partial-fraction decomposition of centrifugal 1/x singularity into lowered moment M_{-1} (algebraic, DLMF 18.9.13) + Stieltjes integral J (three-term recurrence). Single transcendental seed e^a┬ĘEŌéü(a); all other elements algebraic. Associated basis converges faster than ordinary for m=1 (stable by N=10). (Track J, v2.0.10) |
| Separation parameter c┬▓ | numerical-required | Iterative root-finding (Brent method) for self-consistency between angular and radial equations |
| Coupled-channel ceiling | characterized | Error floor 0.19-0.20% from adiabatic approximation; algebraic convergence ~l_maxŌü╗┬▓; 3 channels sufficient; n_basis and R-grid converged. Sub-0.1% requires non-adiabatic (2D variational) solver. (v2.0.8) |

### Level 4 (Mol-Frame Hyperspherical ŌĆö HŌéé)

| Matrix Element | Status | Notes |
|:---------------|:------:|:------|
| Hyperradial overlap (S) | algebraic | Same Laguerre three-term recurrence as Level 3. Pentadiagonal M2 moment matrix. (Track I, v2.0.10) |
| Hyperradial kinetic (K) | algebraic | Same derivative kernel as Level 3. Tridiagonal expansion. (Track I, v2.0.10) |
| Hyperradial potential (U_eff) | numerical-required | Adiabatic curve from angular sweep. ╬╝(Žü) is piecewise-smooth in Žü (NOT algebraic ŌĆö split-region Legendre expansion creates kinks at min/max boundaries). Structurally different from Level 3. (Track S, v2.0.13) |
| Angular eigenvalue sweep (FD) | numerical-required | Point-by-point diagonalization of H_ang at ~130 Žü-values. FD: 1000├Ś1000 matrices, 99% of wall time. Structurally irreducible: no global P(Žü,╬╝)=0 exists (Track S). |
| Angular eigenvalue sweep (spectral) | numerical-required | Jacobi polynomial basis: 50├Ś50 matrices, 269├Ś speedup, ~50% of wall time. SO(6) Casimir free spectrum + precomputed V_ee coupling. `angular_method='spectral'`. Optimal approach given Track S's structural finding. (Track K, v2.0.11) |
| 2D tensor product assembly | numerical-required | H_ang evaluated at each quadrature point for (R_e, ╬▒) tensor product. Dense kronecker assembly. |
| Nuclear coupling (split-region Legendre) | algebraic | Gaunt integrals, exact via 3j triangle inequality (Paper 15). |
| Cusp factor f(╬▒) | negative result | Alpha-only cusp factor f(╬▒) = 1 + (R_e/2)sin(2╬▒) does not improve D_e. Cusp is 2D in (╬▒, ╬ĖŌéüŌéé), not separable in ╬▒ alone. Slow convergence dominated by ╬ĖŌéüŌéé Gegenbauer expansion. (Track U, v2.0.14) |
| 1/rŌéüŌéé graph absorption | structural obstruction | Cannot absorb 1/rŌéüŌéé into conformally weighted SŌüĄ Laplacian. Green's function singularity mismatch: 1/d┬│ (SŌüĄ) vs 1/d┬╣ (Coulomb). Cusp is an embedding exchange constant. (Track W, v2.0.14) |
| Cusp energy correction | corrective (post-processing) | Schwartz partial-wave extrapolation: ╬öE_cusp ~ -A/(l_max+2)Ōü┤. A = (10/ŽĆ)Ō¤©╬┤┬│(rŌéüŌéé)Ō¤®. He: 0.10% at l_max=2 (from 0.24%). HŌéé: R-dependent, ~1.7 mHa differential, ~1.0 pp D_e. Basis-dependent, not exchange constant. (Track X, v2.0.14) |

### Level 4N (Full N-Electron Mol-Frame Hyperspherical ŌĆö LiH)

| Matrix Element | Status | Notes |
|:---------------|:------:|:------|
| SO(12) Casimir eigenvalues | algebraic | Exact from SO(3N) representation theory. Free spectrum validated. (Track AK, v2.0.20) |
| SŌéä Young projector | algebraic | Character-based projection onto [2,2] singlet irrep. Optimized channel-space eigendecompose. (Track AJ, v2.0.20) |

| Cross-pair V_ee (hyperangular) | numerical-required | 3D numerical hyperangular integration. Žü-independent (precomputed once). (Track AK, v2.0.20) |
| Angular eigenvalue sweep | numerical-required | Point-by-point diagonalization at each Žü. Spectral basis: 750 dim at l_max=2 (1000├Ś compression from FD). (Track AK, v2.0.20) |
| Hyperradial solve | numerical-required | Same Laguerre spectral basis as Level 4. (Track AJ, v2.0.20) |

### Level 5 (Composed Geometries ŌĆö LiH, BeHŌéé, HŌééO)

| Matrix Element | Status | Notes |
|:---------------|:------:|:------|
| Z_eff screening function | algebraic | Laguerre spectral expansion: n(r) projected onto L_k(2╬▓r)┬Ęr┬▓┬Ęe^{-2╬▓r} basis. N_core(r) = C_inf ŌłÆ e^{-X}┬ĘP(X), single transcendental seed e^{-2╬▓r}. Production default `zeff_method='spectral_laguerre'`. Auto-fallback to spline for ZŌēź4 (polynomial cancellation). (Track N, v2.0.12; Track R wiring, v2.0.13) |
| Slater F^k integrals | algebraic | Two implementations: (1) Laguerre moment decomposition (Track O, v2.0.12): F^k = c_A^T ┬Ę R^k ┬Ę c_B, single transcendental seed ╬│(1,x). (2) Hypergeometric R^k evaluator (v2.8.1, threshold-dispatched in 2026-05-08 cleanup): `geovac/hypergeometric_slater.py` with exact Fraction-arithmetic for arbitrary n_max. `compute_rk_float()` is correct at all n via threshold dispatch ŌĆö n Ōēż 4 uses the fast pure-float path (machine precision, ~240 ╬╝s/call, bit-identical to pre-fix), n Ōēź 5 delegates to `compute_rk_algebraic` (exact Fraction) and casts to float. **Pre-fix the float path silently degraded for n Ōēź 6** (rel err 1e-7 at n=6, 1e-4 at n=8, 0.2 at n=10, fully wrong sign at n Ōēź 12) due to catastrophic cancellation between O(10^25) Laguerre-product terms summing to O(10^11) ŌĆö exceeded float64 mantissa. Post-fix performance for uncached calls: n=8: 0.54 s, n=10: 1.9 s, n=12: 6.5 s, n=20: ~1 min; cached via `_CACHE_FLOAT` so paid once per unique quartet. `k > l_a + l_b` Gaunt-violating quartets (which `two_electron_integral` filters at the `k_min/k_max` step) now raise a clear `ValueError` instead of crashing on factorial-of-negative. 38 regression tests in `tests/test_hypergeometric_slater.py` cover n=6..20 across ssss/pppp/spsp/mixed quartets, verified against `compute_rk_exact` ground truth. Validated 144/145 table entries in `casimir_ci.py`; found+fixed F┬▓(2p,2p) typo (43/512ŌåÆ45/512). Corrected systematic grid bias (0.06-0.44% per integral). 8x speedup over grid quadrature for small n; large-n cached-Fraction-cast for correctness. Production default for graph-native CI. |
| Phillips-Kleinman PK | algebraic | Ab initio from core eigenvector projection (Paper 17 Sec IV). Gaussian PK parameters A, B from core screening. |
| Inter-fiber exchange coupling | algebraic | Full 1-RDM exchange via channel overlap S(R) and Slater F^0 (algebraic Laguerre). Bond-bond coupling validated (~0.5 Ha). Lone pair coupling disabled at Z_eff>4 (physics limitation). |
| Cross-center V_ne (multipole) | algebraic | Exact termination at L = 2*l_max by Gaunt selection rules. 33 terms at n_max=2, 168 at n_max=3. m-diagonal. Analytical evaluation via incomplete gamma functions (machine precision, zero quadrature). Replaces grid-based trapezoid. (Track CD, v2.0.39-40) |

### Level 5 ŌĆö Spin-ful composed (Tier 2)

| Matrix Element | Status | Notes |
|:---------------|:------:|:------|
| Szmytkowski angular Žā┬Ęr╠é, J┬▓, L┬ĘS, L┬▓, Žā┬▓ | algebraic | Exact eigenvalues in (╬║, m_j); integer / half-integer Kronecker deltas |
| Diagonal hydrogenic Ō¤©r^kŌ¤®, Ō¤©1/r^kŌ¤® | algebraic | Bethe-Salpeter rationals; Ō¤©1/rŌ¤®=Z/n┬▓, Ō¤©1/r┬│Ō¤®=Z┬│/[n┬│l(l+┬Į)(l+1)] (Z┬│ diverges l=0, suppressed by Kramers) |
| Off-diagonal Ō¤©n'l'\|r^k\|n lŌ¤® | algebraic | Direct sympy integration of assoc_laguerre; ~0.1ŌĆō1s per call |
| Breit-Pauli H_SO in (╬║, m_j) | algebraic | Closed form H_SO = ŌłÆZŌü┤╬▒┬▓(╬║+1)/[4n┬│l(l+┬Į)(l+1)], diagonal; exact Kramers at l=0 |
| jj-coupled angular coefficient X_k(╬║_a, m_a, ╬║_c, m_c) | algebraic | sympy wigner_3j, cached, full-Gaunt selection |
| Spinor composed two-body ERI | algebraic | X_k┬ĘX_k┬ĘR^k factorization, radial via hypergeometric_slater (exact Fraction or machine-float) |
| Relativistic ╬│ = ŌłÜ(1ŌłÆ(Z╬▒)┬▓) | algebraic | Degree-2 algebraic over ŌäÜ(╬▒┬▓) via ╬│┬▓ + (Z╬▒)┬▓ = 1; reserved symbol in T1/T2, not bound at Tier 2 |
| Dirac-Coulomb radial Ō¤©r^{-1}Ō¤® (all states) | algebraic | Hellmann-Feynman: Z(╬│n_r+╬║┬▓)/(╬│N_D┬│), exact for all n_r. NR limit Z/n┬▓. (T7, v2.12.0) |
| Dirac-Coulomb radial Ō¤©r^{-2}Ō¤®, Ō¤©r^{-3}Ō¤® (n_r=0) | algebraic | Pochhammer ratios from single-term wavefunction structure. (T7, v2.12.0) |
| Dirac-Coulomb radial Ō¤©r^{-2}Ō¤® (all states) | algebraic | Kramers-Pasternak direct integration via confluent hypergeometric polynomial expansion. Works for all n_r, all ╬║. (v2.18.1) |
| Dirac-Coulomb radial Ō¤©r^{-3}Ō¤® (|╬║|Ōēź2) | algebraic | Kramers-Pasternak direct integration. pŌéü/Ōéé (|╬║|=1, n_rŌēź1) limitation: sympy integral does not converge for near-singular integrand. (v2.18.1) |
| Darwin + mass-velocity ╬▒Ōü┤ corrections | algebraic | Closed-form rationals in (Z, n, l) times ╬▒┬▓; verified Dirac formula exact. (T8, v2.12.0) |
| Breit retarded radial R^k_BP(nŌéülŌéü,nŌéélŌéé;nŌéālŌéā,nŌéälŌéä) | algebraic | Exact Fraction/sympy arithmetic via r_<^k / r_>^{k+3} kernel; Z┬│ scaling verified; `geovac/breit_integrals.py`. (v2.18.0) |
| Seeley-DeWitt coefficients aŌéĆ, aŌéü, aŌéé on S┬│ | algebraic | Exact sympy Rational on unit S┬│ (aŌéĆ=aŌéü=ŌłÜŽĆ, aŌéé=ŌłÜŽĆ/8). `geovac/qed_vacuum_polarization.py`. (v2.18.2) |
| QED vertex even/odd Dirac split D_even(s), D_odd(s) | algebraic | Exact Hurwitz zeta at quarter-integer shifts: D_even via ╬Č(s,3/4), D_odd via ╬Č(s,5/4). At s=4: D_even = ŽĆ┬▓/2 ŌłÆ ŽĆŌü┤/24 ŌłÆ 4G + 4╬▓(4), D_odd = ŽĆ┬▓/2 ŌłÆ ŽĆŌü┤/24 + 4G ŌłÆ 4╬▓(4). PSLQ-verified at 80 digits. `geovac/qed_vertex.py`. (v2.19.1) |
| Screened Ō¤©1/r┬│Ō¤® from FrozenCore Z_eff(r) | numerical-required | Radial Schrodinger equation with Z_eff(r)/r potential solved on uniform grid (FD, eigh_tridiagonal). Ō¤©1/r┬│Ō¤® = Ōł½\|u\|┬▓/r┬│ dr from normalized wavefunction. Enhancement 12-144├Ś over hydrogenic at Z_eff=2 for Ca/Sr/Ba 2p. `geovac/neon_core.py` (screened_r3_inverse, screened_xi_so). (v2.19.4) |
